```python
            # 不应该到这里，但以防递归
            return JSONResponse(
                status_code=500,
                content={
                    "code": ErrorCode.INTERNAL_ERROR,
                    "message": "未知内部错误",
                    "detail": {},
                    "trace_id": trace_id,
                },
            )

        logger.critical(
            "Unhandled exception",
            extra={
                "code": ErrorCode.INTERNAL_ERROR,
                "exception_type": type(exc).__name__,
                "exception_msg": str(exc),
                "trace_id": trace_id,
                "path": request.url.path,
                "method": request.method,
                "stack_trace": traceback.format_exc(),
            },
        )

        return JSONResponse(
            status_code=500,
            content={
                "code": ErrorCode.INTERNAL_ERROR,
                "message": "服务器内部错误，请稍后重试",
                "detail": {"exception_id": trace_id},
                "trace_id": trace_id,
            },
        )
```

### 12.5 业务异常用法示例

```python
# 文件: app/routers/projects.py（示例）

from app.errors.codes import ErrorCode
from app.errors.exceptions import (
    AppError, NotFoundError, ConflictError, RateLimitError, ValidationError
)

# ── 简单检查 ──
async def get_project_or_404(project_id: str, user_id: str):
    project = await db.projects.find_by_id(project_id)
    if not project:
        raise NotFoundError(
            message="项目不存在",
            detail={"project_id": project_id}
        )
    if project.owner_id != user_id:
        raise AppError(
            code=ErrorCode.PROJECT_ACCESS_DENIED,
            message="无权访问此项目",
            detail={"project_id": project_id}
        )
    return project


# ── 冲突检查 + 幂等性 ──
async def confirm_chapter(project_id: str, chapter_id: str, nonce: str):
    # 幂等性检查：用 nonce 防重复提交
    existing = await redis.get(f"nonce:{nonce}")
    if existing:
        raise ConflictError(
            message="该请求已被处理",
            detail={"nonce": nonce, "existing_result": existing}
        )

    chapter = await db.chapters.find_by_id(chapter_id)
    if not chapter:
        raise NotFoundError(
            message="章节不存在",
            detail={"chapter_id": chapter_id}
        )
    if chapter.status == "confirmed":
        raise ConflictError(
            code=ErrorCode.CHAPTER_ALREADY_CONFIRMED,
            message="章节已确认，不可重复操作",
            detail={"chapter_id": chapter_id, "chapter_number": chapter.number}
        )

    # 记录 nonce（有效期 1 小时）
    await redis.setex(f"nonce:{nonce}", 3600, chapter_id)
    # 执行业务逻辑...


# ── 限流 ──
async def check_generation_rate(user_id: str):
    key = f"rate:generate:{user_id}"
    current = await redis.incr(key)
    if current == 1:
        await redis.expire(key, 60)  # 60 秒窗口
    if current > 5:  # 每分钟最多 5 次
        raise RateLimitError(
            message="生成操作过于频繁，请稍后重试",
            detail={"limit": 5, "window_seconds": 60},
            retry_after=30,
        )


# ── Phase 4 写锁 ──
async def acquire_vault_write_lock(project_id: str):
    locked = await redis.set(
        f"phase4:{project_id}:vault_version",
        "1",
        nx=True,
        ex=10  # 10 秒自动释放
    )
    if not locked:
        raise AppError(
            code=ErrorCode.VAULT_WRITE_LOCKED,
            message="世界设定正在同步，请稍候重试",
            detail={"retry_after_ms": 2000, "project_id": project_id}
        )
```

### 12.6 结构化日志记录规范

每个错误日志记录以下标准字段集：

```yaml
# 结构化日志 Schema（JSON 格式）
error_log_entry:
  required:
    timestamp: ISO8601             # 日志时间戳
    level: "ERROR|WARNING|CRITICAL"  # 日志级别
    service: str                   # 服务名称（moling-api / moling-worker）
    trace_id: str                  # 分布式追踪 ID（UUID v4）
    code: int                      # 错误码
    message: str                   # 错误消息
    path: str                      # 请求路径
    method: str                    # HTTP 方法

  optional:
    span_id: str                   # 链路 Span ID
    user_id: str                   # 用户 ID（如有认证）
    project_id: str                # 项目 ID
    request_id: str                # 请求 ID
    detail: dict                   # 错误详情
    exception_type: str            # 异常类名
    exception_msg: str             # 异常消息
    stack_trace: str               # 堆栈信息（仅 5xx）
    duration_ms: float             # 请求耗时
    db_query_count: int            # 请求中 DB 查询次数
    llm_model: str                 # 使用的 LLM 模型
    llm_duration_ms: float         # LLM 调用耗时
    celery_task_id: str            # Celery 任务 ID
    validation_errors: list        # 校验错误列表
    client_ip: str                 # 客户端 IP
    user_agent: str                # UA 信息
    version: str                   # API 版本
```

```python
# 文件: app/core/logging.py

import logging
import json
import uuid
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from pythonjsonlogger import jsonlogger  # pip install python-json-logger


class StructuredFormatter(jsonlogger.JsonFormatter):
    """结构化 JSON 日志格式化器"""

    def add_fields(self, log_record, record, message_dict):
        super().add_fields(log_record, record, message_dict)
        log_record["timestamp"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
        log_record["service"] = "moling-api"
        if "level" not in log_record:
            log_record["level"] = record.levelname
        if "trace_id" not in log_record:
            log_record["trace_id"] = ""  # 会在中间件中填充


def get_error_logger() -> logging.Logger:
    """获取错误日志记录器"""
    logger = logging.getLogger("moling.error")
    logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)

    if not logger.handlers:
        handler = logging.StreamHandler()
        formatter = StructuredFormatter(
            fmt="%(timestamp)s %(level)s %(name)s %(message)s"
        )
        handler.setFormatter(formatter)
        logger.addHandler(handler)

    return logger


# ── 日志配置（logging_config.yaml 对应）──
"""
version: 1
disable_existing_loggers: false
formatters:
  structured:
    (): app.core.logging.StructuredFormatter
    format: "%(timestamp)s %(level)s %(name)s %(message)s"

handlers:
  console:
    class: logging.StreamHandler
    formatter: structured
    stream: ext://sys.stdout

  error_file:
    class: logging.handlers.RotatingFileHandler
    formatter: structured
    filename: /var/log/moling/error.log
    maxBytes: 104857600  # 100MB
    backupCount: 10
    level: ERROR

loggers:
  moling:
    level: INFO
    handlers: [console, error_file]
    propagate: false
  moling.error:
    level: INFO
    handlers: [console, error_file]
    propagate: false
  sqlalchemy.engine:
    level: WARNING
    handlers: [console]
    propagate: false

root:
  level: INFO
  handlers: [console]
"""
```

### 12.7 告警规则

基于错误码分级的告警规则定义：

| 告警级别 | 触发条件 | 响应时间 | 通知渠道 | 示例 |
|---------|---------|---------|---------|------|
| **P0（严重）** | 5xxxx 连续 5 次/分钟 | 15 分钟 | 电话 + 钉钉/企微 | DB 连接失败、LLM 网关不可达 |
| **P1（高）** | 5xxxx 出现一次 | 30 分钟 | 钉钉/企微 + 邮件 | LLM 超时、Phase 4 执行失败 |
| **P2（中）** | 4xxxx 异常率 > 5% | 2 小时 | 钉钉/企微 | 参数校验大量失败 |
| **P3（低）** | 单类错误持续增长趋势 | 24 小时 | 邮件 | 特定资源未找到增多 |

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/monitoring/prometheus-alerts.yml

groups:
  - name: moling-error-alerts
    rules:
      # ── P0: 服务不可用 ──
      - alert: DatabaseConnectionFailure
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"5000[1-2]"}[1m]) > 0.08
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: critical
          pagerduty: moling-production
        annotations:
          summary: "数据库连接异常（{{ $value | humanize }} req/s）"
          description: "错误码 50001/50002 速率超过阈值，可能影响所有读写请求"

      - alert: LLMGatewayUnavailable
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"5020[0-2]"}[1m]) > 0.05
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: critical
        annotations:
          summary: "LLM 网关不可达"
          description: "LiteLLM 代理或底层模型提供商返回错误"

      - alert: RedisConnectionFailure
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"5000[3-4]"}[1m]) > 0.08
        for: 1m
        labels:
          severity: critical
        annotations:
          summary: "Redis 连接异常"

      # ── P1: 服务能力下降 ──
      - alert: HighLLMTimeoutRate
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"5040[1-2]"}[5m]) > 0.1
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: high
        annotations:
          summary: "LLM 超时率过高（{{ $value | humanize }}）"
          description: "LLM 超时错误在 5 分钟内超过 0.1 req/s"

      - alert: HighInternalErrorRate
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"500[0-9]"}[5m]) > 0.05
        for: 3m
        labels:
          severity: high
        annotations:
          summary: "服务端错误率过高"
          description: "5xx 错误速率超过 0.05 req/s，持续 3 分钟"

      # ── P2: 客户端异常上升 ──
      - alert: ElevatedClientErrorRate
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"4[0-9]{4}"}[5m]) > 0.2
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: medium
        annotations:
          summary: "客户端错误率上升"
          description: "4xx 错误速率超过 0.2 req/s，可能为客户端兼容性问题"

      - alert: RateLimitHitHard
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"429[0-9]"}[5m]) > 0.5
        for: 2m
        labels:
          severity: medium
        annotations:
          summary: "大量请求被限流"
          description: "429 限流错误较多，可能需要调整限流参数或扩容"

      # ── P3: 趋势告警 ──
      - alert: NotFoundTrendUp
        expr: predict_linear(rate(moling_errors_total{code=~"404[0-9]"}[30m])[5m], 3600) > 0.1
        labels:
          severity: low
        annotations:
          summary: "404 错误预测上升趋势"
          description: "预计未来 1 小时内 404 错误将达到 0.1 req/s"

      - alert: VaultWriteLockHigh
        expr: rate(moling_errors_total{code="40901"}[5m]) > 0.3
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: low
        annotations:
          summary: "四库写锁冲突频繁"
          description: "四库写入锁冲突过多，可能需要优化锁粒度"
```

```yaml
# AlertManager 通知配置（告警 -> 通知路由）
route:
  receiver: "default"
  group_by: ["alertname", "severity"]
  group_wait: 10s
  group_interval: 30s
  repeat_interval: 4h

  routes:
    - match:
        severity: critical
      receiver: "pager+im"
      repeat_interval: 15m

    - match:
        severity: high
      receiver: "im+email"
      repeat_interval: 30m

    - match:
        severity: medium
      receiver: "im"
      repeat_interval: 2h

    - match:
        severity: low
      receiver: "email"
      repeat_interval: 24h

receivers:
  - name: "pager+im"
    pagerduty_configs:
      - routing_key: "${PAGERDUTY_KEY}"
        severity: "critical"
    webhook_configs:
      - url: "https://qyapi.weixin.qq.com/cgi-bin/webhook/send?key=${WECHAT_BOT_KEY}"
        send_resolved: true

  - name: "im+email"
    webhook_configs:
      - url: "https://qyapi.weixin.qq.com/cgi-bin/webhook/send?key=${WECHAT_BOT_KEY}"
        send_resolved: true
    email_configs:
      - to: "ops@moling.com"

  - name: "im"
    webhook_configs:
      - url: "https://qyapi.weixin.qq.com/cgi-bin/webhook/send?key=${WECHAT_BOT_KEY}"
        send_resolved: true

  - name: "email"
    email_configs:
      - to: "ops@moling.com"
```

### 12.8 客户端重试策略

| 错误码 | 可重试 | 建议等待 | 重试次数上限 | 说明 |
|--------|-------|---------|------------|------|
| 42900–42999 | 是 | Retry-After 头字段 | 3 | 限流，等待后重试 |
| 50000–50099 | 是 | 指数退避（1s, 2s, 4s） | 3 | 服务端内部错误 |
| 50200–50299 | 是 | 5s（可配置） | 2 | 上游服务错误 |
| 50300–50399 | 是 | Retry-After 或 10s | 3 | 服务暂时不可用 |
| 50400–50499 | 是 | 指退避（2s, 4s, 8s） | 3 | 上游超时 |
| 40000–40099 | 否 | — | 0 | 请求参数错误，需修改请求 |
| 40100–40107 | 否（重认证后） | — | 0 | 需刷新令牌或重新登录 |
| 40300–40305 | 否 | — | 0 | 权限不足 |
| 40400–40411 | 否 | — | 0 | 资源不存在 |
| 40900–40909 | 视情况 | 1s–5s | 1 | 冲突，部分可重试 |

```python
# 客户端重试实现示例（Python requests + urllib3）

import time
import random
from typing import Optional

import requests
from requests.adapters import HTTPAdapter
from urllib3.util.retry import Retry


def create_moling_client(base_url: str, api_key: str) -> requests.Session:
    """创建墨灵 API 客户端，带自动重试逻辑"""
    session = requests.Session()
    session.headers.update({
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json",
    })

    def parse_retry_after(response) -> Optional[int]:
        retry_after = response.headers.get("Retry-After")
        if retry_after:
            try:
                return int(retry_after)
            except ValueError:
                return None
        return None

    def backoff(attempt: int, base: float = 1.0, max_delay: float = 30.0) -> float:
        delay = base * (2 ** attempt) + random.uniform(0, 0.5)
        return min(delay, max_delay)

    def retryable_status_code(code: int) -> bool:
        """判断 HTTP 状态码是否可重试"""
        return code in {429, 500, 502, 503, 504}

    class MolingRetry(Retry):
        def __init__(self, *args, **kwargs):
            super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)

        def increment(self, *args, **kwargs):
            resp = kwargs.get("response")
            if resp and resp.status_code == 429:
                retry_after = parse_retry_after(resp)
                if retry_after and retry_after > self.get_backoff_time():
                    # 如果有 Retry-After，使用该值
                    time.sleep(retry_after)
                else:
                    time.sleep(backoff(self.total - kwargs.get("attempt", 0)))
            elif resp and resp.status_code >= 500:
                time.sleep(backoff(self.total - kwargs.get("attempt", 0)))
            return super().increment(*args, **kwargs)

    retry_strategy = MolingRetry(
        total=3,                          # 总重试次数
        connect=2,                         # 连接失败重试
        read=2,                            # 读取超时重试
        backoff_factor=1,                  # 基础退避因子
        status_forcelist=[429, 500, 502, 503, 504],
        allowed_methods=["GET", "POST", "PUT", "DELETE"],
        raise_on_status=True,
    )

    adapter = HTTPAdapter(max_retries=retry_strategy)
    session.mount("https://", adapter)
    session.mount("http://", adapter)

    return session
```

### 12.9 错误码版本管理与废弃策略

```python
# 文件: app/errors/deprecation.py

from enum import IntEnum
from typing import Optional
from datetime import datetime, timezone


class ErrorCodeLifecycle:
    """错误码生命周期管理"""

    @dataclass
    class ErrorCodeMeta:
        code: int
        name: str
        introduced_version: str      # 首次引入版本
        deprecated_version: Optional[str] = None  # 标记废弃的版本
        removed_version: Optional[str] = None     # 移除版本
        superseded_by: Optional[int] = None       # 替代错误码
        description: str = ""

    _registry: dict[int, ErrorCodeMeta] = {}

    @classmethod
    def register(cls, meta: ErrorCodeMeta) -> None:
        cls._registry[meta.code] = meta

    @classmethod
    def is_deprecated(cls, code: int) -> bool:
        meta = cls._registry.get(code)
        if not meta:
            return False
        return meta.deprecated_version is not None

    @classmethod
    def is_removed(cls, code: int, current_version: str) -> bool:
        meta = cls._registry.get(code)
        if not meta or not meta.removed_version:
            return False
        return cls._compare_versions(current_version, meta.removed_version) >= 0

    @classmethod
    def get_migration_path(cls, code: int) -> Optional[int]:
        """获取错误码的迁移路径"""
        meta = cls._registry.get(code)
        if meta and meta.superseded_by:
            return meta.superseded_by
        return None

    @classmethod
    def _compare_versions(cls, v1: str, v2: str) -> int:
        parts1 = [int(x) for x in v1.split(".")]
        parts2 = [int(x) for x in v2.split(".")]
        for a, b in zip(parts1, parts2):
            if a != b:
                return 1 if a > b else -1
        return len(parts1) - len(parts2)


# ── 错误码注册 ──
ErrorCodeLifecycle.register(ErrorCodeLifecycle.ErrorCodeMeta(
    code=50003, name="PHASE4_FAILED",
    introduced_version="1.0.0",
    deprecated_version="1.2.0",
    superseded_by=50403,
    description="被 PHASE4_TIMEOUT 和 PHASE4_STATE_INVALID 替代"
))
```

**错误码废弃流程：**

```
v1.0.0 → 引入错误码
v1.2.0 → 标记为 deprecated（代码中保留，文档标注警告）
v1.3.0 → 新错误码上线（旧码仍返回，但 detail 中带 deprecation_warning）
v2.0.0 → 移除旧错误码（返回 50000: INTERNAL_ERROR，detail 标注已废弃）
```

**API 响应中的废弃提示：**

```python
# 当返回已废弃的错误码时，附加 deprecation 信息
response = {
    "code": 50003,  # 已废弃的错误码
    "message": "PHASE4_FAILED is deprecated",
    "detail": {
        "deprecation": {
            "deprecated_since": "1.2.0",
            "will_be_removed_in": "2.0.0",
            "use_instead": 50403,
            "use_instead_name": "PHASE4_TIMEOUT"
        }
    },
    "trace_id": "xxx"
}
```

### 12.10 分布式追踪（Trace ID）

```python
# 文件: app/core/tracing.py

import uuid
from contextvars import ContextVar
from typing import Optional

from fastapi import Request

# 每一单请求的上下文变量
trace_id_var: ContextVar[str] = ContextVar("trace_id", default="")
span_id_var: ContextVar[str] = ContextVar("span_id", default="")


def generate_trace_id() -> str:
    """生成全局唯一 Trace ID（UUID v4）"""
    return uuid.uuid4().hex


def generate_span_id() -> str:
    """生成 Span ID（8 字节十六进制）"""
    return uuid.uuid4().hex[:16]


def set_trace_id(trace_id: str) -> None:
    trace_id_var.set(trace_id)


def set_span_id(span_id: str) -> None:
    span_id_var.set(span_id)


def get_trace_id(request: Request = None) -> str:
    """获取当前请求的 Trace ID"""
    # 优先从请求头获取（上游服务的追踪上下文）
    if request:
        trace_id = request.headers.get("X-Trace-ID") or \
                   request.headers.get("X-Request-ID") or \
                   request.headers.get("uber-trace-id")
        if trace_id:
            return trace_id
    return trace_id_var.get() or generate_trace_id()


def get_span_id() -> str:
    return span_id_var.get() or generate_span_id()
```

```python
# 文件: app/middleware/tracing.py

from fastapi import Request
from starlette.middleware.base import BaseHTTPMiddleware

from app.core.tracing import generate_trace_id, generate_span_id, set_trace_id, set_span_id


class TracingMiddleware(BaseHTTPMiddleware):
    """分布式追踪中间件：为每个请求注入 Trace ID"""

    async def dispatch(self, request: Request, call_next):
        # 从请求头读取或生成 Trace ID
        trace_id = request.headers.get("X-Trace-ID") or generate_trace_id()
        span_id = generate_span_id()

        set_trace_id(trace_id)
        set_span_id(span_id)

        # 注入响应头
        response = await call_next(request)
        response.headers["X-Trace-ID"] = trace_id
        return response
```

```python
# FastAPI 应用注册

from app.middleware.error_handler import setup_error_handlers
from app.middleware.tracing import TracingMiddleware

app = FastAPI(title="墨灵 API", version="1.0.0")

# 顺序：Tracing → 其他中间件 → Error Handlers
app.add_middleware(TracingMiddleware)
setup_error_handlers(app)
```

**Trace ID 传递规范：**

| 场景 | 传递方式 | 示例 |
|------|---------|------|
| HTTP 请求 | Header: `X-Trace-ID` | `X-Trace-ID: a1b2c3d4e5f6...` |
| Celery 任务 | 任务参数 | `task.apply_async(args=[], headers={"trace_id": trace_id})` |
| 异步消息 | Header 或消息属性 | 同上 |
| 日志 | `trace_id` 字段 | `{"trace_id": "xxx", "level": "ERROR", ...}` |
| LLM 调用 | LiteLLM 的 metadata | `litellm.call(metadata={"trace_id": trace_id})` |
| 客户端响应 | 响应 Header | `X-Trace-ID: xxx` |

**Celery 任务 Trace ID 传递：**

```python
# 文件: app/tasks/base.py

from celery import Task as CeleryTask
from app.core.tracing import trace_id_var, generate_trace_id


class TraceAwareTask(CeleryTask):
    """支持 Trace ID 传递的 Celery 任务基类"""

    def apply_async(self, args=None, kwargs=None, **options):
        # 从当前上下文获取 trace_id
        trace_id = trace_id_var.get() or generate_trace_id()
        headers = options.pop("headers", {})
        headers["trace_id"] = trace_id
        return super().apply_async(args, kwargs, headers=headers, **options)

    def __call__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        # 从任务头中提取 trace_id
        request_headers = getattr(self.request, "headers", {}) or {}
        trace_id = request_headers.get("trace_id") or generate_trace_id()
        trace_id_var.set(trace_id)
        return super().__call__(*args, **kwargs)
```

---



## 十三、性能目标与扩容

### 13.1 RED 方法监控指标体系

墨灵采用 **RED 方法**（Rate / Error / Duration）定义核心监控指标。每个服务组件都需要覆盖这三个维度。

| 服务组件 | Rate（请求率） | Error（错误率） | Duration（延迟） | 关键 SLI |
|---------|---------------|----------------|-----------------|---------|
| FastAPI（API 网关） | requests/sec | 4xx / 5xx 占比 | P50 / P95 / P99 | P99 < 500ms（非 LLM） |
| Celery Worker | tasks/sec | task_failure 占比 | task_duration | Phase 4 P99 < 6s |
| PostgreSQL | queries/sec | error_count | query_duration | P99 < 200ms |
| Redis | ops/sec | error_count | cmd_duration | P99 < 10ms |
| LiteLLM Proxy | tokens/sec | error_count | first_token_latency | P95 < 2s |
| 对象存储 | uploads + downloads/sec | error_count | throughput MB/s | P99 < 1s |

#### 13.1.1 性能 SLI / SLO 定义

| 接口 | SLI 指标 | SLO（月度目标） | 测量器 |
|------|---------|----------------|--------|
| GET /projects | P95 延迟 < 150ms | 99.9% | Grafana |
| GET /vault/* | P95 延迟 < 200ms | 99.5% | Grafana |
| POST /redraw | P95 延迟 < 80ms | 99.9% | Grafana |
| POST /generate | P95 延迟 < 12s | 99.0% | Grafana |
| POST /confirm | P95 延迟 < 200ms | 99.9% | Grafana |
| Phase 4（async） | P95 延迟 < 3.5s | 99.5% | Celery Flower |
| GET /cards/pool | P95 延迟 < 150ms | 99.9% | Grafana |
| POST /import（60章） | P50 耗时 < 2min | 99.0% | Grafana |
| 整体 API 可用性 | HTTP 200 占比 | 99.95% | Blackbox Exporter |

#### 13.1.2 详细延迟目标

| 接口 | P50 | P95 | P99 | 超时设置（LB） | 备注 |
|------|-----|-----|-----|--------------|------|
| GET /projects | 50ms | 150ms | 300ms | 5s | 缓存命中率 > 90% |
| GET /vault/* | 80ms | 200ms | 400ms | 5s | 摘要缓存 |
| POST /redraw | 30ms | 80ms | 150ms | 3s | 纯 DB 操作 |
| POST /generate | 8s | 12s | 18s | 30s | LLM 调用，流式响应 |
| POST /confirm | 100ms | 200ms | 500ms | 5s | 含 Phase 4 写锁 |
| Phase 4（async） | 2s | 3.5s | 6s | 30s | 含 LLM 调用 |
| GET /cards/pool | 50ms | 150ms | 300ms | 5s | 带缓存 |
| POST /import（60章） | 2min | 3min | 5min | 10min | 批量 LLM 调用 |

### 13.2 Prometheus 指标定义

```python
# 文件: app/monitoring/metrics.py

from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram, Gauge, Summary
from prometheus_fastapi_instrumentator import Instrumentator

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 1. HTTP 请求指标（FastAPI Instrumentator 自动生成）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 标准指标（Instrumentator 默认会生成这些）:
#   - http_request_duration_seconds: {method, path, status} 直方图
#   - http_requests_total: {method, path, status} 计数器

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 2. 业务指标
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# 错误计数（按错误码细分）
errors_total = Counter(
    "moling_errors_total",
    "Total errors by error code",
    ["code", "service", "model"],  # model: LLM 模型名（可选）
)

# 生成请求耗时（细粒度分桶）
generation_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_generation_duration_seconds",
    "Generation request duration in seconds",
    ["model", "mode"],  # mode: generate / redraw / confirm / phase4
    buckets=(1, 2, 4, 6, 8, 10, 12, 15, 18, 20, 25, 30, 40, 60, float("inf")),
)

# LLM Token 消耗
llm_token_total = Counter(
    "moling_llm_tokens_total",
    "Total LLM tokens consumed",
    ["model", "provider", "operation"],  # operation: generate / phase4 / import / redraw
)

# LLM 首次延迟
llm_first_token_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_llm_first_token_seconds",
    "LLM first token latency",
    ["model", "provider"],
    buckets=(0.1, 0.25, 0.5, 0.75, 1, 2, 3, 5, 10, float("inf")),
)

# LLM 调用总延迟
llm_total_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_llm_total_duration_seconds",
    "LLM total call duration (including streaming)",
    ["model", "provider"],
    buckets=(1, 2, 4, 6, 8, 10, 12, 15, 20, 25, 30, 40, 50, 60, float("inf")),
)

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

db_pool_overflow = Gauge("moling_db_pool_overflow", "DB connection pool overflow")

    "moling_celery_queue_depth",
    "Celery task queue depth",
    ["queue"],  # queue: phase4 / import / default
)

# 缓存命中率
cache_hits_total = Counter("moling_cache_hits_total", "Cache hits", ["cache_name"])
cache_misses_total = Counter("moling_cache_misses_total", "Cache misses", ["cache_name"])

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 4. 瓶颈监控指标
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# SQL 慢查询计数
slow_queries_total = Counter(
    "moling_slow_queries_total",
    "Slow SQL queries (>200ms)",
    ["query_signature"],
)

# 数据库连接等待时间
db_acquire_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_db_acquire_seconds",
    "Time to acquire a DB connection from pool",
    buckets=(0.001, 0.005, 0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5, 1, float("inf")),
)

# Redis 操作延迟
redis_cmd_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_redis_cmd_seconds",
    "Redis command duration",
    ["command"],
    buckets=(0.001, 0.002, 0.005, 0.01, 0.02, 0.05, 0.1, float("inf")),

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

# Phase 4 执行计数器

    "moling_phase4_total",
    "Phase 4 execution results",
    ["status"],  # status: success / failure / timeout
)

# 卡牌抽取数
card_draws_total = Counter("moling_card_draws_total", "Total card draws", ["rarity"])


# ── FastAPI 指标初始化 ──
def setup_metrics(app):
    """初始化 Prometheus 指标采集"""
    Instrumentator().instrument(app).expose(app, endpoint="/metrics")
```
