#### 13.2.1 Grafana 面板设计

建议创建以下 Grafana Dashboard：

**面板 1：API 概览（Moling API Overview）**
```
Row: ["HTTP Rate", "Error Rate", "Avg Duration"]
  ├── HTTP Requests Rate (rps) — 时间序列图，按 method + path 着色
  ├── Error Rate (4xx / 5xx)  — 时间序列图，按 status 分组
  ├── P50 / P95 / P99 Latency — 时间序列图，按 endpoint 分组
  ├── Error Code 分布          — 饼图/柱状图
  └── 健康检查状态             — 状态面板（up/down）
```

**面板 2：LLM 性能（LLM Performance）**
```
Row: ["Latency", "Token Usage", "Error Rate"]
  ├── Generation Duration P50/P95/P99 — 按 model 分组
  ├── First Token Latency P95         — 按 provider 分组
  ├── Tokens Per Minute               — 堆叠面积图，按 model 分组
  ├── LLM Error Rate                  — 按 model 分组
  └── LLM Cost ($/hour)               — 估算成本（基于 token 用量 * 单价）
```

**面板 3：基础设施（Infrastructure）**
```
Row: ["DB", "Redis", "Celery"]
  ├── DB Connection Pool (active/idle/waiting)
  ├── Slow Query Count / 5min
  ├── Redis Hit Rate (%)
  ├── Redis Command Latency P99
  ├── Celery Queue Depth（phase4 / import / default）
  └── Celery Worker Utilization (%)
```

**面板 4：业务 KPI（Business KPI）**
```
Row: ["Generation", "Cards", "Users"]
  ├── Daily Active Users (DAU)
  ├── Generations / hour
  ├── Phase 4 Success Rate (%)
  ├── Phase 4 Duration P95
  ├── Card Draw Rate / hour
  └── Import Job Completion Rate (%)
```

### 13.3 缓存策略

#### 13.3.1 缓存层级架构

```
┌─────────────┐     L1: Local Memory Cache（进程内）
│   L1 Cache  │     - 热点数据，< 1KB 响应
│ (进程内存)  │     - TTL 极短（5–30s）
└──────┬──────┘     - 不跨节点共享
       │
┌──────▼──────┐     L2: Redis 分布式缓存
│  L2 Cache   │     - 共享数据，所有节点可见
│   (Redis)   │     - TTL 中等（30s–1h）
└──────┬──────┘     - 支持主动失效（publish/subscribe）
       │
┌──────▼──────┐     L3: LLM 语义缓存
│  L3 Cache   │     - 基于 embedding 相似度匹配
│ (LLM Cache) │     - 仅对确定性的小模型请求
└─────────────┘     - LiteLLM 的 caching=True
```

#### 13.3.2 详细缓存配置

| 数据 | 缓存层级 | TTL | 失效策略 | 预估大小 | 命中率目标 |
|------|---------|-----|---------|---------|-----------|
| 项目列表（用户） | L2 Redis | 5min | 写入失效（publish） | 100KB/用户 | > 90% |
| 项目详情 | L2 Redis | 5min | 写入失效 | 10KB/项目 | > 85% |
| 四库摘要 | L2 Redis | 1min | 定时失效 | 50KB/项目 | > 90% |
| 卡牌池（活跃） | L2 Redis | 1min | 抽牌/重绘时失效 | 100KB/项目 | > 80% |
| LLM 小模型结果 | L2 + L3 | 1h | 基于 embedding 相似度 | 可变 | > 60% |
| 动态层 | — | 不缓存 | — | — | 0%（直接读 DB） |
| Phase 4 状态 | L2 Redis | — | 实时写入 | 1KB/项目 | 实时 |
| 用户 Session | L2 Redis | 24h | 主动失效（登出） | 1KB/用户 | > 99% |
| 配置/元数据 | L1 内存 + L2 | 5min | 轮询刷新 | < 1KB | > 99% |

#### 13.3.3 缓存穿透/击穿/雪崩防护

```python
# 文件: app/core/cache.py

import asyncio
import hashlib
import random
from typing import Optional, Callable, Awaitable, Any, TypeVar

from redis.asyncio import Redis

T = TypeVar("T")


class CacheProtection:
    """缓存防护策略集合"""

    # ── 缓存穿透防护（布隆过滤器 / 空值缓存）──
    @staticmethod
    async def anti_penetration(
        redis: Redis,
        key: str,
        fetch_func: Callable[[], Awaitable[Optional[T]]],
        ttl: int = 300,
        empty_ttl: int = 30,  # 空值缓存时间（防穿透）
    ) -> Optional[T]:
        """带穿透防护的缓存读取

        当查询结果为空时，仍缓存空标记，用于防缓存穿透。
        """
        cached = await redis.get(key)
        if cached is not None:
            if cached == b"__NULL__":
                return None
            return deserialize(cached)

        value = await fetch_func()
        if value is None:
            # 缓存空标记（较短 TTL）
            await redis.setex(key, empty_ttl, b"__NULL__")
        else:
            await redis.setex(key, ttl, serialize(value))
        return value

    # ── 缓存击穿防护（互斥锁）──
    @staticmethod
    async def anti_breakdown(
        redis: Redis,
        key: str,
        fetch_func: Callable[[], Awaitable[T]],
        ttl: int = 300,
        lock_ttl: int = 5,  # 互斥锁 TTL
        retry_delay: float = 0.1,
        max_retries: int = 10,
    ) -> T:
        """带互斥锁的缓存重建（防击穿）

        高并发场景下缓存失效时，只有一个请求重建缓存，
        其他请求等待或返回旧数据。
        """
        cached = await redis.get(key)
        if cached is not None:
            return deserialize(cached)

        lock_key = f"{key}:lock"
        for attempt in range(max_retries):
            acquired = await redis.set(lock_key, "1", nx=True, ex=lock_ttl)
            if acquired:
                try:
                    # 再次检查缓存（双重检测）
                    cached = await redis.get(key)
                    if cached is not None:
                        return deserialize(cached)

                    value = await fetch_func()
                    await redis.setex(key, ttl, serialize(value))
                    return value
                finally:
                    await redis.delete(lock_key)
            else:
                # 等待其他请求重建缓存
                await asyncio.sleep(retry_delay * (attempt + 1))

        # 退避：直接查 DB（不缓存）
        return await fetch_func()

    # ── 缓存雪崩防护（随机 TTL + 预热）──
    @staticmethod
    def jitter_ttl(base_ttl: int, jitter_ratio: float = 0.1) -> int:
        """在基础 TTL 上加入随机抖动，防止批量缓存同时过期"""
        jitter = int(base_ttl * jitter_ratio * random.random())
        return base_ttl + jitter

    @classmethod
    async def set_with_jitter(
        cls, redis: Redis, key: str, value: Any,
        base_ttl: int, jitter_ratio: float = 0.1,
    ) -> None:
        """写入带随机 TTL 抖动的缓存"""
        ttl = cls.jitter_ttl(base_ttl, jitter_ratio)
        await redis.setex(key, ttl, serialize(value))

    # ── 缓存预热接口 ──
    @staticmethod
    async def warm_up(
        redis: Redis,
        keys_func: Callable[[], Awaitable[list[str]]],
        fetch_func: Callable[[str], Awaitable[Optional[T]]],
        ttl: int,
        batch_size: int = 10,
    ) -> int:
        """批量预热缓存

        在服务启动或数据变更后调用。
        Returns: 成功预热的条目数
        """
        keys = await keys_func()
        warmed = 0
        for i in range(0, len(keys), batch_size):
            batch = keys[i:i + batch_size]
            tasks = []
            for key in batch:
                value = await fetch_func(key)
                if value is not None:
                    await redis.setex(key, ttl, serialize(value))
                    warmed += 1
            await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
        return warmed
```

### 13.4 数据库索引优化

```sql
-- 覆盖索引（减少回表）
CREATE INDEX idx_chapters_project_status
  ON chapters(project_id, chapter_number, status)
  INCLUDE (title, word_count, created_at);

CREATE INDEX idx_chapters_user_feed
  ON chapters(user_id, updated_at DESC)
  WHERE status = 'confirmed';

-- 部分索引（只索引活跃卡牌）
CREATE INDEX idx_cards_pool_active
  ON card_pool(project_id, last_drawn_chapter NULLS FIRST)
  WHERE is_active = true;

-- 复合索引（四库查询）
CREATE INDEX idx_vault_entries
  ON vault_entries(project_id, category, created_at DESC);

-- Gin 全文搜索
CREATE INDEX idx_projects_search
  ON projects USING gin(to_tsvector('simple', title || ' ' || author || ' ' || description));

-- 生成任务状态索引
CREATE INDEX idx_generation_jobs_status
  ON generation_jobs(project_id, status, created_at DESC);

-- Phase 4 锁状态索引
CREATE INDEX idx_phase4_status
  ON phase4_jobs(project_id, status, created_at DESC);
```

### 13.5 SQL 慢查询监控与优化

```python
# 文件: app/monitoring/slow_query.py

import time
import hashlib
import logging
from typing import Callable

from sqlalchemy import event
from sqlalchemy.engine import Engine
from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram

logger = logging.getLogger("moling.slow_query")

# 慢查询指标
slow_query_counter = Counter(
    "moling_slow_queries_total",
    "Slow SQL queries > threshold",
    ["query_signature", "operation"],
)

query_duration = Histogram(
    "moling_query_duration_seconds",
    "SQL query duration",
    ["operation"],
    buckets=(0.001, 0.005, 0.01, 0.025, 0.05, 0.1, 0.2, 0.5, 1, 2, 5, float("inf")),
)


def query_signature(sql: str) -> str:
    """生成 SQL 查询签名（归一化参数）"""
    # 移除具体参数值，保留模板
    import re
    normalized = re.sub(r"'[^']*'", "?", sql)
    normalized = re.sub(r"\b\d+\b", "?", normalized)
    return hashlib.md5(normalized.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]


@event.listens_for(Engine, "before_cursor_execute")
def before_cursor_execute(conn, cursor, statement, parameters, context, executemany):
    """查询执行前记录开始时间"""
    conn.info.setdefault("query_start_time", {})
    conn.info["query_start_time"][cursor] = time.perf_counter()


@event.listens_for(Engine, "after_cursor_execute")
def after_cursor_execute(conn, cursor, statement, parameters, context, executemany):
    """查询执行后记录耗时"""
    start = conn.info["query_start_time"].get(cursor)
    if start is None:
        return

    duration = time.perf_counter() - start
    sig = query_signature(statement)

    # 判断是否为 SELECT（用于 operation 分类）
    op = statement.strip().split()[0].upper() if statement.strip() else "UNKNOWN"

    query_duration.labels(operation=op).observe(duration)

    # 慢查询告警（> 200ms）
    if duration > 0.2:
        slow_query_counter.labels(query_signature=sig, operation=op).inc()

        logger.warning(
            "Slow SQL query detected",
            extra={
                "query_signature": sig,
                "duration_ms": round(duration * 1000, 2),
                "operation": op,
                "statement": statement[:500],  # 截断长 SQL
                "parameters": str(parameters)[:200],
            },
        )

    # 移除记录
    conn.info["query_start_time"].pop(cursor, None)


# ── 慢查询优化流程 ──
"""
慢查询处理 SOP：

1. 发现阶段
   - Prometheus 告警 "moling_slow_queries_total > 0" 触发
   - 开发者查看对应 query_signature

2. 分析阶段
   - 在数据库执行: EXPLAIN (ANALYZE, BUFFERS) <SQL>
   - 检查：Seq Scan / 索引选择 / 行估算偏差

3. 优化阶段
   - 添加或修改索引
   - 重写查询（避免 N+1、减少 JOIN、使用覆盖索引）
   - 添加物化视图（针对复杂聚合查询）

4. 验证阶段
   - 重新 EXPLAIN ANALYZE 确认
   - 观察 Prometheus 指标确认下降

5. 长期监控
   - 新增查询需 review 执行计划
   - CI 中集成 pgbadger 静态分析
"""
```

### 13.6 连接池配置

```python
# 文件: app/core/pool_config.py

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 数据库连接池（asyncpg + SQLAlchemy）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

DATABASE_POOL_CONFIG = {
    # 连接池大小
    "pool_size": 20,           # 最小连接数
    "max_overflow": 10,        # 最大额外连接数（峰值时扩展）
    "pool_timeout": 30,        # 获取连接的等待超时（秒）
    "pool_recycle": 3600,      # 连接回收时间（秒），防止长时间空闲断开
    "pool_pre_ping": True,     # 每次取出连接前执行 ping 检查

    # 语句执行超时
    "query_timeout": 30,       # SQL 执行超时（秒）
    "statement_cache_size": 500,  # SQL 语句缓存（避免重复 prepare）
    "max_cached_statement_lifetime": 300,  # 缓存语句生存时间（秒）
}

# 计算公式（MaxThreads × (CPUCores × 2 + EffectiveSpindleCount)）
# 对于 FastAPI + async workers（Uvicorn）:
# 推荐 pool_size = workers × 2（每个 worker 维持 2 个连接）
# 例如 4 workers → pool_size = 8，但考虑预留，设为 20


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# Redis 连接池
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

REDIS_POOL_CONFIG = {
    "max_connections": 50,     # Redis 连接池上限
    "timeout": 5,              # 获取连接超时（秒）
    "retry_on_timeout": True,  # 超时是否重试
    "health_check_interval": 30,  # 健康检查间隔（秒）
    "socket_keepalive": True,  # TCP keepalive
    "socket_connect_timeout": 5,  # 连接超时（秒）
    "socket_timeout": 10,      # 读写超时（秒）
}

# 配置多 DB 实例：
# - DB 0: 缓存（无需持久化，允许丢失）
# - DB 1: Celery 消息 + 结果（持久化 + AOF）
# - DB 2: Session + 锁 + 实时状态（持久化 + AOF）


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# HTTP 连接池（httpx / aiohttp）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

HTTP_CLIENT_CONFIG = {
    "timeout": {
        "connect": 5,          # 连接超时
        "read": 30,            # 读取超时（LLM 流式可能需要更大）
        "write": 10,           # 写入超时
        "pool": 30,            # 等待池连接的超时
    },
    "limits": {
        "max_connections": 100,   # 总连接数上限
        "max_keepalive_connections": 20,  # 保持活跃连接数
        "keepalive_expiry": 30,   # 保持活跃连接超时（秒）
    },
    "retries": 2,              # 重试次数
    "verify": True,            # TLS 证书验证
}


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 池状态监控 & 动态调整（见 monitoring/pool_watcher.py）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

async def report_pool_stats():
    """定时上报连接池状态"""
    # DB: SELECT count(*) FROM pg_stat_activity WHERE state = 'active'
    # Redis: INFO CLIENTS -> connected_clients
    # HTTP: client._pool._available_connections
    pass
```

### 13.7 水平扩容方案

#### 13.7.1 分层扩容策略

```
扩容阶梯表：
┌─────────────┬────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────┐
│   阶段       │ DAU < 100  │ DAU 100–1K  │ DAU 1K–10K   │ DAU 10K+     │
├─────────────┼────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┤
│ FastAPI     │ 1×4C8G     │ 3×4C8G      │ 6×8C16G      │ 10+×8C16G    │
│ PostgreSQL  │ 1×2C4G     │ 1主2从       │ 3主3从+读写分离 │ Patroni 集群 │
│ Redis       │ 1×1C2G     │ 3节点哨兵    │ 6节点集群     │ 12节点集群    │
│ Celery      │ 1 Worker   │ 3 Workers   │ 10 Workers    │ 20+ Workers   │
│ LiteLLM     │ 1×2C4G     │ 2×2C4G      │ 4×4C8G        │ 8×4C8G+       │
│ 存储        │ MinIO      │ MinIO(3节点) │ S3兼容对象存储 │ CDN+多区域    │
└─────────────┴────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────┘
```

#### 13.7.2 K8s HPA 自动扩容配置

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/k8s/hpa.yaml

---
# ── FastAPI HPA ──
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: moling-api-hpa
  namespace: moling
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: moling-api
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 20
  metrics:
    # CPU 利用率触发扩容
    - type: Resource
      resource:
        name: cpu
        target:
          type: Utilization
          averageUtilization: 70
    # 内存利用率（辅助指标）
    - type: Resource
      resource:
        name: memory
        target:
          type: Utilization
          averageUtilization: 80
    # 自定义指标：请求 QPS
    - type: Pods
      pods:
        metric:
          name: moling_http_requests_per_second
        target:
          type: AverageValue
          averageValue: 200
  behavior:
    scaleUp:
      policies:
        - type: Pods
          value: 2        # 每次最多扩容 2 个 Pod
          periodSeconds: 60
        - type: Percent
          value: 50       # 或者扩展现有 50%
          periodSeconds: 60
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 0      # 立即扩容
      selectPolicy: Max                  # 取宽松策略
    scaleDown:
      policies:
        - type: Pods
          value: 1        # 每次最多缩 1 个 Pod
          periodSeconds: 120
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300    # 稳定窗口 5 分钟（避免抖动）
      selectPolicy: Max

---
# ── Celery Worker HPA ──
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: moling-worker-hpa
  namespace: moling
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: moling-worker
  minReplicas: 1
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
    - type: External
      external:
        metric:
          name: celery_queue_depth
          selector:
            matchLabels:
              queue: phase4
        target:
          type: AverageValue
          averageValue: 20  # 队列深度 > 20 时扩容
  behavior:
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 30
      policies:
        - type: Pods
          value: 2
          periodSeconds: 60
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 180
      policies:
        - type: Pods
          value: 1
          periodSeconds: 120

---
# ── LiteLLM HPA ──
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: moling-litellm-hpa
  namespace: moling
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: moling-litellm
  minReplicas: 1
  maxReplicas: 5
  metrics:
    - type: Resource
      resource:
        name: cpu
        target:
          type: Utilization
          averageUtilization: 60
  behavior:
    scaleUp:
      policies:
        - type: Pods
          value: 1
          periodSeconds: 60
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
      policies:
        - type: Percent
          value: 20
          periodSeconds: 120
```

### 13.8 压测方案

#### 13.8.1 工具选择

| 场景 | 工具 | 原因 |
|------|------|------|
| API 接口压测 | locust / k6 | Python / JavaScript 脚本易于集成 CI |
| 长时间稳定性 | k6 | 低资源，适合 CI |
| LLM 代理压测 | vegeta | 简洁，适合 HTTP 代理层 |
| 数据库压测 | pgbench | PostgreSQL 原生压测工具 |
| 批量任务 | Celery 内置 | 直接监控 task 耗时 |

#### 13.8.2 压测场景设计

```python
# 文件: tests/load/locustfile.py

from locust import HttpUser, task, between, tag
import random


class MolingReadUser(HttpUser):
    """模拟读操作密集型用户"""
    wait_time = between(1, 5)

    @tag("read", "projects")
    @task(3)
    def list_projects(self):
        self.client.get("/api/v1/projects")

    @tag("read", "vault")
    @task(2)
    def get_vault_summary(self):
        project_id = self._pick_project()
        self.client.get(f"/api/v1/projects/{project_id}/vault/summary")

    @tag("read", "cards")
    @task(2)
    def get_card_pool(self):
        project_id = self._pick_project()
        self.client.get(f"/api/v1/projects/{project_id}/cards/pool")

    def _pick_project(self):
        return random.choice(["demo-001", "demo-002", "demo-003"])


class MolingWriteUser(HttpUser):
    """模拟写操作密集型用户（LLM 调用）"""
    wait_time = between(30, 120)  # 低频但重量级

    @tag("write", "generate")
    @task(1)
    def generate_chapter(self):
        self.client.post("/api/v1/generate", json={
            "project_id": "demo-001",
            "mode": "draft",
            "target_word_count": 2000,
        })

    @tag("write", "redraw")
    @task(2)
    def redraw_card(self):
        self.client.post("/api/v1/redraw", json={
            "project_id": "demo-001",
            "card_id": "c-001",
            "reason": "rewrite",
        })

    @tag("write", "confirm")
    @task(1)
    def confirm_chapter(self):
        self.client.post("/api/v1/confirm", json={
            "project_id": "demo-001",
            "chapter_id": "ch-001",
        })
```

```yaml
# k6 压测配置示例（config.yaml）
scenarios:
  constant_load:
    executor: constant-vus
    vus: 50
    duration: 5m

  ramp_up:
    executor: ramping-vus
    start_vus: 0
    stages:
      - duration: 2m
        target: 200
      - duration: 5m
        target: 200
      - duration: 2m
        target: 0

  stress_test:
    executor: ramping-arrival-rate
    start_rate: 10
    time_unit: 1s
    pre_allocated_vus: 50
    stages:
      - duration: 2m
        target: 100
      - duration: 2m
        target: 200
      - duration: 2m
        target: 300
      - duration: 1m
        target: 400
```

#### 13.8.3 性能基准目标

| 压测场景 | 并发数 | 目标 RPS | P95 延迟 | 错误率上限 |
|---------|-------|---------|---------|-----------|
| 纯读场景（GET） | 200 VUs | > 500 | < 200ms | < 0.1% |
| 混合场景（80%读 + 20%写） | 100 VUs | > 200 | < 500ms（读） | < 0.5% |
| 写密集（generate/confirm） | 20 VUs | — | P95 < 12s | < 1% |
| 导入场景（批量） | 5 VUs | — | P50 < 2min | < 2% |
| 长时间稳定（4h） | 50 VUs | > 150 | 无明显衰减 | < 0.5% |
| 尖峰场景（突发 5x） | 500 VUs | — | 限流后 P95 < 30s | < 5%（429） |

### 13.9 LLM 调用延迟特殊处理

```python
# 文件: app/services/llm.py

import asyncio
import time
import logging
from typing import AsyncIterator, Optional, Callable

from prometheus_client import Counter, Histogram

from app.errors.exceptions import LLMTimeoutError, LLMProviderError, RateLimitError
from app.monitoring.metrics import llm_total_duration

logger = logging.getLogger("moling.llm")

# ── 客户端超时 ──
# 不同模型有不同的合理超时
LLM_TIMEOUT_CONFIG = {
    "pro": {     # deepseek-v4-pro（短输出：提取/抽卡/Phase 4）
        "read_timeout": 15,
        "connect_timeout": 5,
        "max_retries": 2,
    },
    "flash": {   # deepseek-v4-flash（长输出：正文写作/头脑风暴）
        "read_timeout": 30,
        "connect_timeout": 5,
        "max_retries": 2,
    },
}


class LLMService:
    """LLM 调用服务，含超时、重试、降级"""

    def __init__(self, gateway_url: str, client: httpx.AsyncClient):
        self.gateway_url = gateway_url
        self.client = client

    async def generate(
        self,
        prompt: str,
        model_tier: str = "medium",
        streaming: bool = True,
        trace_id: Optional[str] = None,
        fallback_model: Optional[str] = None,
    ) -> AsyncIterator[str]:
        """带降级和超时控制的 LLM 调用"""
        timeout_config = LLM_TIMEOUT_CONFIG.get(model_tier, LLM_TIMEOUT_CONFIG["medium"])

        # 重试逻辑
        last_error = None
        for attempt in range(timeout_config["max_retries"] + 1):
            try:
                # 带超时的 HTTP 调用
                async with asyncio.timeout(timeout_config["read_timeout"]):
                    response = await self._do_generate(
                        prompt=prompt,
                        model_tier=model_tier,
                        streaming=streaming,
                        trace_id=trace_id,
                    )
                    return response

            except asyncio.TimeoutError as e:
                last_error = e
                logger.warning(
                    "LLM call timeout",
                    extra={
                        "model_tier": model_tier,
                        "attempt": attempt + 1,
                        "timeout": timeout_config["read_timeout"],
                        "trace_id": trace_id,
                    },
                )
                if attempt < timeout_config["max_retries"]:
                    await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # 指数退避
                    continue

                # 最后一次重试也超时 → 降级
                if fallback_model:
                    logger.info(
                        "Falling back to model",
                        extra={
                            "from_tier": model_tier,
                            "to_model": fallback_model,
                            "trace_id": trace_id,
                        },
                    )
                    return await self.generate(
                        prompt=prompt,
                        model_tier=model_tier,
                        streaming=streaming,
                        fallback_model=None,  # 只降级一次
                    )
                raise LLMTimeoutError(detail={"model_tier": model_tier})

            except httpx.HTTPStatusError as e:
                if e.response.status_code == 429:
                    raise RateLimitError(
                        message="LLM 调用频率超限",
                        retry_after=int(e.response.headers.get("Retry-After", 30)),
                    )
                elif 500 <= e.response.status_code < 600:
                    last_error = e
                    if attempt < timeout_config["max_retries"]:
                        await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)
                        continue
                raise LLMProviderError(
                    detail={"status": e.response.status_code, "model_tier": model_tier}
                )

            except Exception as e:
                last_error = e
                if attempt < timeout_config["max_retries"]:
                    await asyncio.sleep(2 ** attempt)
                    continue
                raise LLMProviderError(detail={"exception": str(e)})

    async def _do_generate(self, prompt, model_tier, streaming, trace_id):
        """实际调用 LiteLLM 代理"""
        model_map = {
            "pro": os.getenv("LLM_PRO_MODEL", "deepseek-v4-pro"),
            "flash": os.getenv("LLM_FLASH_MODEL", "deepseek-v4-flash"),
        }
        model = model_map.get(model_tier)
        start = time.perf_counter()

        response = await self.client.post(
            f"{self.gateway_url}/chat/completions",
            json={
                "model": model,
                "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                "stream": streaming,
                "metadata": {"trace_id": trace_id, "service": "moling-api"},
            },
        )
        response.raise_for_status()
        duration = time.perf_counter() - start
        llm_total_duration.labels(model=model, provider="litellm").observe(duration)

        logger.info(
            "LLM call completed",
            extra={
                "model": model,
                "duration_ms": round(duration * 1000, 2),
                "trace_id": trace_id,
            },
        )
        return response


# ── 队列机制（防止 LLM 调用过载）──

class LLMRateLimiter:
    """LLM 调用速率限制器（令牌桶）"""

    def __init__(self, rate: int = 10, burst: int = 20):
        self.rate = rate          # 每秒允许的请求数
        self.burst = burst        # 突发容量
        self._semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(burst)
        self._tokens = burst
        self._last_refill = time.monotonic()
        self._lock = asyncio.Lock()

    async def acquire(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> bool:
        """获取调用许可（带超时）"""
        try:
            async with asyncio.timeout(timeout):
                async with self._semaphore:
                    await self._wait_for_token()
                    return True
        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
            return False

    async def _wait_for_token(self):
        """等待令牌可用"""
        while True:
            async with self._lock:
                now = time.monotonic()
                elapsed = now - self._last_refill
                self._tokens = min(self.burst, self._tokens + elapsed * self.rate)
                self._last_refill = now

                if self._tokens >= 1:
                    self._tokens -= 1
                    return

            await asyncio.sleep(0.05)


# ── 降级策略配置 ──

LLM_DEGRADATION_CONFIG = {
    "timeout_fallback": {
        "description": "超时后使用备用模型重试（flash→pro）",
        "action": "error → pro 模型 → 返回结果",
    },
    "model_downgrade": {
        "description": "flash 模型负载高时使用 pro 模型",
        "condition": "flash_queue_depth > 10",
        "action": "return_pro_model_result",
    },
    "semantic_cache_override": {
        "description": "LLM 不可用时返回语义缓存",
        "condition": "all_providers_unavailable",
        "action": "return_cached_or_stale",
    },
    "circuit_breaker": {
        "description": "LLM 错误率超 50% 时熔断 30s",
        "threshold": 0.5,
        "window": 60,
        "cooldown": 30,
        "action": "reject_immediately → 返回 503",
    },
}
```

---
### 13.5 连接池与 PgBouncer 配置

#### 连接池架构总览

合理的连接池架构采用三层模型，每层解决不同粒度的连接复用问题：

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│         应用层连接池 (SQLAlchemy)             │
│                                               │
│  作用：减少应用内部重复创建连接的 TCP 开销     │
│  粒度：进程级别，每个 worker 独立管理          │
│  池大小：pool_size=10, max_overflow=5         │
│           ↓                                  │
│  每个 worker 最多持有 15 个前端连接            │
│  4 workers × 15 = 60 个前端连接               │
└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────┘
                   │
                   ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│         PgBouncer (事务级连接复用)            │
│                                               │
│  作用：将大量前端连接收敛为少量后端连接         │
│  粒度：全局级别，独立进程管理                  │
│  池大小：default_pool_size=25                 │
│           ↓                                  │
│  60 个前端连接 → 收敛至 25 个后端连接          │
│  连接复用率 ≈ 2.4:1                          │
└──────────────────┬──────────────────────────┘
                   │
                   ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│         PostgreSQL (固定连接数)               │
│                                               │
│  作用：维持稳定且可控的连接负载                │
│  后端连接：25 常规 + 5 预留 = 30 最大        │
│  预留容量：50%+ 给维护/备份/监控使用          │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### SQLAlchemy 连接池配置

应用层使用 SQLAlchemy 异步引擎，配置连接池参数：

```python
# app/core/database.py

from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import create_async_engine, AsyncSession
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
from app.core.config import settings

engine = create_async_engine(
    settings.DATABASE_URL,
    
    # 连接池大小
    pool_size=10,             # 池中保持的常驻连接数
    max_overflow=5,           # 池耗尽后额外创建的最大连接数（峰值突发）
                              # 总最大连接 = pool_size + max_overflow = 15
    
    # 连接健康检查
    pool_pre_ping=True,       # 每次从池中取出连接时执行 SELECT 1 验证
    
    # 连接回收
    pool_recycle=3600,        # 连接使用 3600 秒（1 小时）后被回收重建
                              # 防止 long-lived 连接被数据库侧断开
    
    # 连接池预热
    pool_size=10,             # 应用启动时即创建 10 个连接（惰性创建）
    
    # 等待策略
    pool_timeout=30,          # 等待空闲连接的超时时间（秒）
                              # 超过则抛出 TimeoutError
    
    # 日志
    echo=False,               # 生产环境关闭 SQL 日志
    
    # PgBouncer 兼容（见 14.2.1）
    connect_args={
        "prepared_statement_cache_size": 0,
        "statement_cache_size": 0,
    },
)

AsyncSessionLocal = sessionmaker(
    engine,
    class_=AsyncSession,
    expire_on_commit=False,
)
```

**参数含义详解**：

| 参数 | 值 | 说明 |
|------|-----|------|
| `pool_size` | 10 | 连接池常驻连接数。4 workers × 10 = 40，通过 PgBouncer 收敛至 25 |
| `max_overflow` | 5 | 突发流量时额外创建最多 5 个连接，峰值后回收 |
| `pool_pre_ping` | True | 每次从池中取出连接前执行 `SELECT 1` 检查，防止使用已断开的连接 |
| `pool_recycle` | 3600 | 避免 PostgreSQL `statement_timeout` 或防火墙断开空闲连接 |
| `pool_timeout` | 30 | 池中无空闲连接时的最大等待时间，超过则报错 |

#### 不同场景的连接数计算

| 阶段 | DAU | 在线并发 | Worker数 | 应用连接 | PgBouncer | 推荐方案 |
|------|-----|---------|---------|---------|-----------|---------|
| 开发调试 | 1-10 | < 5 | 1 | 10-15 | 无需 | 直连 PostgreSQL，`max_connections=50` |
| 小规模 | 100 | 20-30 | 2 | 20-30（可选配 PgBouncer） | 可选 | 直连 + 增大 `max_connections=50` |
| 中等规模 | 500 | 100-150 | 4 | 40-60 | 推荐部署 | PgBouncer + `default_pool_size=15` |
| 企业规模 | 1000 | 200-300 | 4 | 60-80 | 必须部署 | PgBouncer + `default_pool_size=25` |

**详细计算过程（1000 DAU 示例）**：

```
应用层连接数：
  FastAPI Workers:      4 × (10 + 5)   = 60 连接
  Celery Workers:       2 × (8 + 2)    = 20 连接
  管理/迁移/健康检查:                    5 连接
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  总前端连接:                             85 连接

PgBouncer 收敛后：
  default_pool_size:    25 连接
  reserve_pool_size:     5 连接
  ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  总后端连接（对 PostgreSQL）:             30 连接

PostgreSQL 连接容量：
  max_connections:      100 连接
  实际需求:              30 连接
  预留余量:              70 连接（留给 VACUUM, 备份, 监控, 临时查询）
```

#### PgBouncer 资源配置建议

**单实例资源配置**：

| DAU | vCPU | 内存 | 网络 | 连接数 |
|-----|------|------|------|--------|
| ≤ 500 | 0.25 | 128 MB | 100 Mbps | ≤ 100 |
| 1000 | 0.5 | 256 MB | 1 Gbps | 200 |
| 5000 | 1 | 512 MB | 1 Gbps | 500 |

PgBouncer 资源需求极低，CPU 和内存开销远低于 PostgreSQL 自身。在 1000 DAU 场景下，PgBouncer 的 CPU 使用率通常 < 5%，内存 < 50 MB。

**高可用方案**：

单点 PgBouncer 可能成为瓶颈或故障点。在 1000+ DAU 场景推荐以下方案：

```
方案 A：双实例 + DNS 轮询（推荐）
┌─────────┐    ┌──────────────┐
│ 客户端 1 │───→│ pgbouncer-01 │
├─────────┤    ├──────────────┤
│ 客户端 2 │───→│ pgbouncer-02 │
├─────────┤    ├──────────────┤
│ 客户端 N │───→│ DNS 轮询     │──→ pgbouncer-01 / pgbouncer-02
└─────────┘    └──────────────┘    │
                                    ├──→ PostgreSQL (Primary)
                                    │
                              Patroni 自动故障转移


方案 B：Kubernetes Service（云原生）
┌───────────┐     ┌─────────────────────────┐
│ Pod: app   │────→│ Kubernetes Service:      │
│ Pod: app   │────→│ pgbouncer.svc.cluster.local:6432
│ Pod: worker│────→│ 后端: pgbouncer-0,1 (StatefulSet)
└───────────┘     └─────────────────────────┘
```

**与 Patroni 的配合**：

在 Patroni 管理的高可用 PostgreSQL 集群中，PgBouncer 应感知主从切换：

```yaml
# docker-compose 中 PgBouncer 与 Patroni 配合
pgbouncer:
  image: edoburu/pgbouncer:1.22
  environment:
    DB_HOST: patroni-proxy  # 指向 Patroni 的负载均衡器或 haproxy
    DB_PORT: "5000"          # Patroni 写入端口的默认值
  # PgBouncer 不感知主从切换，由 Patroni/haproxy 自动路由
```

或者使用 `auto_host` 模式配合 etcd/Consul 动态发现主节点。更简单的做法是在 Patroni 前部署 haproxy，PgBouncer 指向 haproxy 的写入端口，haproxy 由 Patroni 自动配置主从路由。

**经验法则**：

1. **优先配池，再配库**：先规划好连接池大小，再设定 `max_connections`，不要让 PostgreSQL 承受未经控制的连接数
2. **PgBouncer 应有监控告警**：`SHOW STATS` 的 `total_wait_time` 是衡量连接压力的核心指标
3. **预留连接给 DBA**：PostgreSQL 中预留 `superuser_reserved_connections = 10`，确保紧急维护可连接
4. **连接池不是性能银弹**：连接池解决的是连接数控制问题，不是查询性能问题。查询慢仍需从索引、SQL 优化、缓存等方向解决


---




## 十四、部署架构

### 14.1 Docker 多阶段构建

```dockerfile
# 文件: Dockerfile

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 第一阶段：依赖编译（基于 Python 3.12 slim）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
FROM python:3.12-slim AS builder

WORKDIR /build

# 安装编译依赖
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    gcc \
    libpq-dev \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# 利用 Docker 层缓存：只在 requirements 变化时重新安装
COPY requirements.txt .
RUN pip install --user --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt

COPY requirements-dev.txt .
RUN pip install --user --no-cache-dir -r requirements-dev.txt || true

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 第二阶段：运行时镜像（最小多阶段）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
FROM python:3.12-slim AS runtime

# 创建非 root 用户
RUN groupadd -r moling && useradd -r -g moling -d /app -s /sbin/nologin moling

# 系统依赖（仅运行时）
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    libpq5 \
    curl \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

WORKDIR /app

# 从 builder 阶段复制 Python 包
COPY --from=builder /root/.local /root/.local
ENV PATH=/root/.local/bin:$PATH

# 复制应用代码
COPY alembic.ini .
COPY alembic/ alembic/
COPY app/ app/
COPY scripts/ scripts/

# 权限最小化
RUN chown -R moling:moling /app && \
    chmod -R 750 /app && \
    chmod 640 /app/alembic.ini

USER moling

# 健康检查
HEALTHCHECK --interval=10s --timeout=5s --start-period=30s --retries=3 \
    CMD curl -f http://localhost:8000/health || exit 1

EXPOSE 8000

# 默认启动命令（可由 docker-compose 覆盖）
CMD ["uvicorn", "app.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000", \
     "--workers", "4", "--proxy-headers", "--forwarded-allow-ips", "*"]


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 第三阶段：开发镜像（带热重载）
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
FROM runtime AS dev

USER root
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir watchfiles ipython
USER moling

CMD ["uvicorn", "app.main:app", "--host", "0.0.0.0", "--port", "8000", \
     "--reload", "--reload-dir", "/app/app"]


# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 第二阶段变体：Celery Worker 镜像
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
FROM runtime AS worker

USER moling
CMD ["celery", "-A", "app.tasks.celery_app", "worker", \
     "--loglevel=info", "--concurrency=4", "--max-tasks-per-child=100", \
     "--time-limit=300", "--soft-time-limit=240"]
```

```yaml
# 文件: .dockerignore

__pycache__/
*.pyc
*.pyo
.git/
.gitignore
.env*
*.md
tests/
docs/
.venv/
venv/
.pytest_cache/
.coverage
htmlcov/
```

### 14.2 Docker Compose 开发环境

```yaml
# 文件: docker-compose.yml

version: "3.9"

x-logging: &default-logging
  driver: "json-file"
  options:
    max-size: "10m"
    max-file: "3"

services:
  app:
    build:
      context: .
      target: dev
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    env_file: .env
    depends_on:
      db:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
      litellm:
        condition: service_started
    volumes:
      - ./app:/app/app          # 本地挂载：热重载
      - ./alembic:/app/alembic
      - ./scripts:/app/scripts
    logging: *default-logging

  worker:
    build:
      context: .
      target: worker
    env_file: .env
    depends_on:
      db:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    volumes:
      - ./app:/app/app
    logging: *default-logging

  db:
    image: pgvector/pgvector:pg17
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: moling
      POSTGRES_USER: moling
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: moling_secret
      POSTGRES_INITDB_ARGS: "--data-checksums"  # 数据校验
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init-db.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U moling"]
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 5
    logging: *default-logging

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redisdata:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes --appendfsync everysec
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 3s
      retries: 5
    logging: *default-logging

  litellm:
    image: ghcr.io/berriai/litellm:main-latest
    ports:
      - "4000:4000"
    env_file: .env
    volumes:
      - ./litellm_config.yaml:/app/config.yaml:ro
      - litellm_cache:/app/cache
    command: --config /app/config.yaml --port 4000 --num_workers 4
    logging: *default-logging

  # 开发辅助服务：MinIO 对象存储
  minio:
    image: minio/minio:latest
    ports:
      - "9000:9000"
      - "9001:9001"  # Console
    environment:
      MINIO_ROOT_USER: minioadmin
      MINIO_ROOT_PASSWORD: minioadmin
    volumes:
      - miniodata:/data
    command: server /data --console-address ":9001"
    logging: *default-logging

  # 开发辅助：Redis Commander（Web 管理）
  redis-commander:
    image: rediscommander/redis-commander:latest
    ports:
      - "8081:8081"
    environment:
      REDIS_HOSTS: local:redis:6379

volumes:
  pgdata:
  redisdata:
  miniodata:
  litellm_cache:

### 14.2.1 PgBouncer 连接池代理（1000 DAU 扩展）

#### 为什么需要 PgBouncer

FastAPI 使用 asyncpg 作为 PostgreSQL 异步驱动，默认连接池配置为 10 个连接。在 4 个 Uvicorn worker 的场景下，仅应用层就占据：

- **FastAPI 应用层**：10 连接 × 4 workers = **40 连接**
- **Celery Worker**（2 个进程 × 8 连接池）：~**16 连接**
- **其他服务**（健康检查、迁移脚本、管理工具）：~**5-10 连接**
- **合计**：约 **60-70 个并发连接**

PostgreSQL 默认 `max_connections = 100`，在预留 20-30 个连接给维护操作（VACUUM、备份、监控查询）后，应用层可用额度仅剩 70-80，几乎触碰天花板。

连接数过多的风险：

- **内存膨胀**：每个 PostgreSQL 连接约消耗 5-10 MB（含缓存上下文），100 个连接即占用 500 MB-1 GB，触发 OOM 风险
- **上下文切换开销**：PostgreSQL 是进程模型，过多活跃连接导致 CPU 调度开销剧增
- **连接建立延迟**：频繁创建/销毁连接增加 1-3ms 的握手延迟

**1000 DAU 定量估算**：

| 场景 | 活跃用户占比 | 并发请求 | 需求连接数 |
|------|-------------|---------|-----------|
| API 请求（读写） | 20% 同时在线 | 200 QPS | 30-40 |
| WebSocket/SSE | 10% 长连接 | 100 连接 | 10-15 |
| Celery 任务 | 后台 | 50 TPS | 10-15 |
| 后台管理/报表 | 内部 | 10 QPS | 5-10 |
| **合计** | | | **55-80** |

直接连接 PostgreSQL 需要预留 80+ 连接，而 PgBouncer 可以将实际对 PostgreSQL 的连接数缩减至 **25-30**，释放 60%+ 的数据库连接容量。

#### PgBouncer 配置

以下为 `pgbouncer.ini` 完整配置文件：

```ini
[databases]
moling = host=db port=5432 dbname=moling

[pgbouncer]
listen_addr = 0.0.0.0
listen_port = 6432
auth_type = md5
auth_file = /etc/pgbouncer/userlist.txt

;;; 连接池模式
;; transaction — 事务级复用，最佳性能，支持预处理语句（需设置 max_prepared_statements=0）
;; session — 会话级，兼容性最好但复用度低
;; statement — 语句级，复用度最高但有副作用
pool_mode = transaction

;;; 池大小配置
default_pool_size = 25        ;; 每个用户/数据库对后端连接数
max_client_conn = 200         ;; 最大前端连接数
max_db_connections = 50       ;; 单个数据库最大后端连接数上限
reserve_pool_size = 5         ;; 预留连接（在常规池用满后启用）
reserve_pool_timeout = 3.0    ;; 常规池等3秒无空闲连接后启用保留池

;;; 超时和重试
server_idle_timeout = 300      ;; 后端空闲 5 分钟关闭
client_idle_timeout = 600      ;; 前端空闲 10 分钟断开
client_login_timeout = 30      ;; 登录超时 30 秒
query_timeout = 30             ;; 查询超时 30 秒（避免慢查询拖死连接池）
query_wait_timeout = 10        ;; 等待可用连接的查询超时 10 秒
cancel_wait_timeout = 5        ;; 取消请求等待超时

;;; 连接生命周期
server_lifetime = 3600         ;; 后端连接最长存活 1 小时后被回收
server_connect_timeout = 10    ;; 连接 PostgreSQL 超时 10 秒
server_check_delay = 30        ;; 30 秒检查一次断开的服务器连接

;;; 监控与日志
stats_period = 60              ;; 每 60 秒输出统计信息到日志
log_connections = 1            ;; 记录连接日志（生产环境建议关掉减少日志量）
log_disconnections = 0         ;; 关闭断开日志
verbose = 0                    ;; 日志级别，0=最小，2=最详细

;;; 安全
peer_id = 0                    ;; 禁用 peer_id
ignore_startup_parameters = extra_float_digits  ;; 忽略某些启动参数，避免兼容性问题

;;; TCP 优化
tcp_defer_accept = 1
tcp_socket_buffer = 0
tcp_keepalive = 1
tcp_keepcnt = 3
tcp_keepidle = 60
tcp_keepintvl = 10
```

认证用户文件 `/etc/pgbouncer/userlist.txt`：

```text
"moling" "md5xxxxx..."   ;; 使用 md5 哈希密码，可通过 `echo -n "passwordmoling" | md5sum` 生成
```

生成 md5 哈希的命令：

```bash
# PgBouncer 的 md5 格式是 "md5" + md5(password + username)
echo -n "md5$(echo -n 'your_password_here''moling' | md5sum | cut -d' ' -f1)"
```

#### Docker Compose 集成

在 `docker-compose.yml` 中添加 PgBouncer 服务：

```yaml
version: "3.8"

services:
  # ... 原有服务 ...

  db:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: moling
      POSTGRES_USER: moling
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - pgdata:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U moling -d moling"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5
    restart: unless-stopped

  pgbouncer:
    image: edoburu/pgbouncer:1.22
    ports:
      - "6432:6432"
    environment:
      DB_USER: moling
      DB_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
      DB_HOST: db
      DB_PORT: "5432"
      DB_NAME: moling
      POOL_MODE: transaction
      DEFAULT_POOL_SIZE: "25"
      MAX_CLIENT_CONN: "200"
      AUTH_TYPE: md5
      SERVER_IDLE_TIMEOUT: "300"
      QUERY_TIMEOUT: "30"
      QUERY_WAIT_TIMEOUT: "10"
    volumes:
      - ./docker/pgbouncer/userlist.txt:/etc/pgbouncer/userlist.txt:ro
      - ./docker/pgbouncer/pgbouncer.ini:/etc/pgbouncer/pgbouncer.ini:ro
    depends_on:
      db:
        condition: service_healthy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pgbouncer -u pgbouncer -q /etc/pgbouncer/pgbouncer.ini 2>&1 || pg_isready -h localhost -p 6432"]
      interval: 15s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 10s
    restart: unless-stopped
    networks:
      - app_network

  app:
    build: .
    depends_on:
      pgbouncer:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    # ... 其他配置 ...

  worker:
    build: .
    depends_on:
      pgbouncer:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started
    # ... 其他配置 ...
```

依赖关系拓扑：

```
app ──────┐
          ├──→ pgbouncer ──→ db
worker ───┘
```

#### 连接字符串变更

将所有应用配置中的数据库连接 URL 从直连 PostgreSQL 改为指向 PgBouncer：

| 组件 | 原连接字符串 | 新连接字符串 |
|------|-------------|-------------|
| FastAPI / SQLAlchemy | `postgresql+asyncpg://moling:xxx@db:5432/moling` | `postgresql+asyncpg://moling:xxx@pgbouncer:6432/moling` |
| Celery / psycopg2 | `postgresql://moling:xxx@db:5432/moling` | `postgresql://moling:xxx@pgbouncer:6432/moling` |
| Alembic 迁移 | `postgresql://moling:xxx@db:5432/moling` | `postgresql://moling:xxx@pgbouncer:6432/moling` |

**.env 文件配置变更**：

```bash
# 原配置
DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://moling:${DB_PASSWORD}@db:5432/moling
CELERY_DATABASE_URL=postgresql://moling:${DB_PASSWORD}@db:5432/moling

# 新配置
DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://moling:${DB_PASSWORD}@pgbouncer:6432/moling
CELERY_DATABASE_URL=postgresql://moling:${DB_PASSWORD}@pgbouncer:6432/moling
```

**asyncpg 与 PgBouncer transaction 模式兼容性注意事项**：

1. **预处理语句**：asyncpg 默认使用预处理语句（prepared statements），但 PgBouncer 的 `transaction` 模式下预处理语句无法跨事务复用。解决方法：
   - 设置 `pool_prepared_statement_cache_size=0` 禁用 asyncpg 的预处理语句缓存
   - 或者在 PgBouncer 配置中设置 `max_prepared_statements=0`

2. **`DEALLOCATE ALL`**：建议在连接池回收时发送 `DEALLOCATE ALL` 清理未释放的预处理语句

3. **`LISTEN`/`NOTIFY`**：不支持在 `transaction` 模式下使用 `LISTEN`/`NOTIFY`，如果需要请使用 `session` 模式或直连

4. **临时表**：`transaction` 模式下临时表在事务结束后被清理，如需使用临时表请改用 `session` 模式

SQLAlchemy 异步引擎配置示例（兼容 PgBouncer）：

```python
from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import create_async_engine

engine = create_async_engine(
    "postgresql+asyncpg://moling:password@pgbouncer:6432/moling",
    pool_size=10,
    max_overflow=5,
    pool_pre_ping=True,
    pool_recycle=3600,
    connect_args={
        "prepared_statement_cache_size": 0,  # 禁用预处理语句缓存
        "statement_cache_size": 0,           # 禁用语句缓存
    }
)
```

#### 部署注意事项

**生产部署建议**：

1. **同可用区部署**：PgBouncer 应部署在与 PostgreSQL 相同的节点或同一可用区，网络延迟控制在 1ms 以内，避免引入额外延迟

2. **资源占用**：
   - PgBouncer 是单线程事件驱动模型，CPU 消耗极低（通常 < 5% 单核）
   - 内存占用约 2KB/连接，200 连接仅 ~400KB
   - 推荐配置：0.5 vCPU / 256MB RAM（足够支撑 1000 DAU）

3. **不要部署在应用侧**：PgBouncer 部署在应用侧会引入跨网络延迟，应始终靠近数据库部署

**监控指标**（通过 `SHOW STATS`、`SHOW POOLS`、`SHOW CLIENTS` 命令获取）：

| 指标 | 命令 | 告警阈值 |
|------|------|---------|
| 活跃客户端连接数 | `SHOW CLIENTS` | > 150 告警 |
| 活跃服务端连接数 | `SHOW POOLS` | > 20 告警 |
| 等待队列长度 | `SHOW STATS.total_wait_time` | > 5 秒告警 |
| 查询超时次数 | `SHOW STATS.total_query_timeout_count` | > 10/分钟告警 |
| 连接超时次数 | `SHOW STATS.total_xact_timeout_count` | > 5/分钟告警 |
| 池使用率 | `SHOW POOLS.cl_active / default_pool_size` | > 80% 告警 |

Prometheus 集成可使用 `prometheus_pgbouncer_exporter`。

**PgBouncer 不是连接池替代品**：

```
应用连接池 (SQLAlchemy/asyncpg)
  ├── 作用：减少应用侧连接建立开销
  ├── 管理：应用进程内管理
  └── 策略：按需创建、复用、回收

PgBouncer (中间代理)
  ├── 作用：复用 PostgreSQL 后端连接
  ├── 管理：独立进程管理
  └── 策略：事务级复用，控制对 DB 的连接数
  
两者配合：应用连接池负责应用内部的连接复用，PgBouncer 负责全局连接收敛。
```

**常见陷阱**：

1. **事务未关闭导致连接泄漏**：`transaction` 模式下，长时间未提交/回滚的事务会占用连接，需设置 `query_timeout` 和 `server_idle_timeout`
2. **迁移工具直连**：Alembic 迁移建议直接在 PgBouncer 上运行，但 DDL 操作（如 `ALTER TABLE`）长时间占用连接，建议在低峰期执行或临时使用 session 模式
3. **长查询阻塞池**：单个慢查询会占用一个后端连接，耗尽后其他查询排队等待，需要结合 `pg_stat_activity` 和 PgBouncer `SHOW STATS` 定位

```

### 14.3 生产部署（Kubernetes）

```
完整生产架构：

                               ┌──────────────────────────────┐
                               │       阿里云 SLB / AWS ALB    │
                               │   (TLS Termination + 灰度)    │
                               └──────────────┬───────────────┘
                                              │
                               ┌──────────────▼───────────────┐
                               │    Nginx Ingress Controller   │
                               │   (速率限制 + WAF + 白名单)  │
                               └──┬──────┬──────┬──────┬──────┘
                                  │      │      │      │
                    ┌─────────────┤      │      ├─────────────┐
                    ▼             │      │      │             ▼
            ┌─────────────┐      ▼      ▼      ▼     ┌─────────────┐
            │ Celery       │ ┌─────────────────────┐  │  Grafana /  │
            │ Worker x(N)  │ │   FastAPI Pod x(N)  │  │  Prometheus │
            │ Phase4/Import│ │  (Horizontal Pod    │  │  / Loki     │
            │              │ │   Autoscaling)      │  └─────────────┘
            └──────┬───────┘ └──────────┬──────────┘
                   │                    │
                   └────────────────────┤
                                        │
                   ┌────────────────────▼──────────────────────┐
                   │              Redis Sentinel/Cluster        │
                   │   DB0: Cache  |  DB1: Celery  |  DB2: Sess│
                   └────────────────────┬───────────────────────┘
                                        │
                   ┌────────────────────▼──────────────────────┐
                   │        PostgreSQL (Patroni + HA)          │
                   │           Primary + 2 Replicas            │
                   │         WAL 归档 → S3 (持续归档)         │
                   └────────────────────┬───────────────────────┘
                                        │
                   ┌────────────────────▼──────────────────────┐
                   │          LiteLLM Proxy x(N)               │
                   │   deepseek-v4-pro / deepseek-v4-flash       │
                   └────────────────────┬───────────────────────┘
                                        │
                   ┌────────────────────▼──────────────────────┐
                   │        LLM Providers (OpenAI / Anthropic) │
                   └───────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 14.3.1 K8s 部署清单

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/k8s/namespace.yaml

apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: moling
  labels:
    name: moling
    environment: production
```

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/k8s/deployment-api.yaml

apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: moling-api
  namespace: moling
  labels:
    app: moling
    component: api
spec:
  replicas: 2
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1        # 每次最多额外启动 1 个 Pod
      maxUnavailable: 1   # 最多允许 1 个 Pod 不可用
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: moling
      component: api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: moling
        component: api
    spec:
      # Pod 级别的安全上下文
      securityContext:
        runAsNonRoot: true
        runAsUser: 1001
        fsGroup: 1001
        seccompProfile:
          type: RuntimeDefault

      containers:
      - name: api
        image: registry.moling.com/moling-api:latest
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8000
          protocol: TCP
          name: http

        resources:
          requests:
            cpu: "1"
            memory: "2Gi"
          limits:
            cpu: "4"
            memory: "4Gi"

        envFrom:
        - secretRef:
            name: moling-secrets
        - configMapRef:
            name: moling-config

        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /live
            port: 8000
          initialDelaySeconds: 15
          periodSeconds: 15
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3

        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 8000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          successThreshold: 1
          failureThreshold: 3

        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8000
          initialDelaySeconds: 3
          periodSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 30

        lifecycle:
          preStop:
            exec:
              command: ["/bin/sh", "-c", "sleep 10 && uvicorn --app app.main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8000 --workers 0 --no-server"]

        volumeMounts:
        - name: tmp
          mountPath: /tmp
        - name: cache
          mountPath: /app/cache

      # Pod 反亲和性：不同节点分散部署
      affinity:
        podAntiAffinity:
          preferredDuringSchedulingIgnoredDuringExecution:
          - weight: 100
            podAffinityTerm:
              labelSelector:
                matchExpressions:
                - key: component
                  operator: In
                  values:
                  - api
              topologyKey: kubernetes.io/hostname

      volumes:
      - name: tmp
        emptyDir: {}
      - name: cache
        emptyDir:
          sizeLimit: "1Gi"

      terminationGracePeriodSeconds: 60
```

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/k8s/service.yaml

apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: moling-api
  namespace: moling
  annotations:
    service.beta.kubernetes.io/alibaba-cloud-loadbalancer-protocol: "https"
    service.beta.kubernetes.io/alibaba-cloud-loadbalancer-cert-id: "${CERT_ID}"
spec:
  type: ClusterIP
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: 8000
    protocol: TCP
    name: http
  selector:
    app: moling
    component: api
```

### 14.4 CI/CD 流水线

```yaml
# 文件: .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml

name: Moling CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
    tags: ["v*.*.*"]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

env:
  REGISTRY: registry.moling.com
  IMAGE_NAME: moling-api
  K8S_NAMESPACE: moling
  DEPLOYMENT_NAME: moling-api

jobs:
  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  # 阶段 1: 代码质量检查
  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  lint-and-typecheck:
    name: Lint & Type Check
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.12"
          cache: "pip"
      - run: pip install -r requirements-dev.txt
      - name: Ruff lint
        run: ruff check app/ tests/
      - name: Ruff format
        run: ruff format --check app/ tests/
      - name: Mypy type check
        run: mypy app/ --strict
      - name: Bandit security scan
        run: bandit -r app/ --severity-level high

  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  # 阶段 2: 测试
  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  test:
    name: Unit & Integration Tests
    needs: lint-and-typecheck
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    services:
      postgres:
        image: pgvector/pgvector:pg17
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: testpass
          POSTGRES_DB: moling_test
          POSTGRES_USER: moling
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 5s
          --health-timeout 3s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 5s
          --health-timeout 3s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 6379:6379
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.12"
          cache: "pip"
      - run: pip install -r requirements-dev.txt
      - name: Run unit tests
        run: pytest tests/unit/ -v --cov=app --cov-report=xml --cov-report=term-missing
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql+asyncpg://moling:testpass@localhost:5432/moling_test
          REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379/0
      - name: Run integration tests
        run: pytest tests/integration/ -v
        env:
          DATABASE_URL: postgresql+asyncpg://moling:testpass@localhost:5432/moling_test
          REDIS_URL: redis://localhost:6379/0
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v4

  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  # 阶段 3: 构建 & 推送 Docker 镜像
  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  build-and-push:
    name: Build & Push Docker Image
    needs: test
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' || startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v3
      - name: Log in to container registry
        uses: docker/login-action@v3
        with:
          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
          username: ${{ secrets.REGISTRY_USER }}
          password: ${{ secrets.REGISTRY_PASSWORD }}

      # 生成版本标签
      - name: Generate image tags
        id: meta
        run: |
          SHORT_SHA=${GITHUB_SHA::8}
          if [[ "${{ github.ref }}" == refs/tags/v* ]]; then
            VERSION=${GITHUB_REF#refs/tags/v}
            echo "tags=${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:${VERSION},${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:latest" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
          else
            echo "tags=${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:${SHORT_SHA},${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:main-latest" >> $GITHUB_OUTPUT
          fi

      - name: Build and push
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v5
        with:
          context: .
          target: runtime
          push: true
          tags: |
            ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
          provenance: true
          sbom: true

      - name: Generate SBOM
        uses: anchore/sbom-action@v0
        with:
          image: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:latest

      - name: Vulnerability scan
        uses: aquasecurity/trivy-action@master
        with:
          image-ref: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:latest
          format: table
          exit-code: 1
          severity: HIGH,CRITICAL

  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  # 阶段 4: 部署到 K8s
  # ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  deploy:
    name: Deploy to Kubernetes
    needs: build-and-push
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - name: Set up kubectl
        uses: azure/setup-kubectl@v4
        with:
          version: "latest"
      - name: Configure Kubeconfig
        run: |
          mkdir -p $HOME/.kube
          echo "${{ secrets.KUBE_CONFIG }}" | base64 -d > $HOME/.kube/config
      - name: Update deployment image
        run: |
          SHORT_SHA=${GITHUB_SHA::8}
          kubectl set image deployment/${{ env.DEPLOYMENT_NAME }} \
            -n ${{ env.K8S_NAMESPACE }} \
            api=${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}:${SHORT_SHA}
      - name: Rollout status
        run: |
          kubectl rollout status deployment/${{ env.DEPLOYMENT_NAME }} \
            -n ${{ env.K8S_NAMESPACE }} \
            --timeout=300s
      - name: Run DB migration
        run: |
          kubectl exec deployment/${{ env.DEPLOYMENT_NAME }} \
            -n ${{ env.K8S_NAMESPACE }} \
            -- alembic upgrade head
      - name: Smoke test
        run: |
          sleep 10
          kubectl run smoke-test --image=busybox -n ${{ env.K8S_NAMESPACE }} \
            --rm --restart=Never -- \
            wget -qO- http://moling-api/health
```

### 14.5 健康检查端点

```python
# 文件: app/routers/health.py

import time
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Optional

from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException
from pydantic import BaseModel

from app.core.database import get_db_session
from app.core.cache import get_redis

logger = logging.getLogger("moling.health")

router = APIRouter(tags=["health"])


class HealthStatus(BaseModel):
    status: str                   # "healthy" | "degraded" | "unhealthy"
    version: str
    timestamp: str
    uptime_seconds: float
    checks: dict[str, "ComponentHealth"]


class ComponentHealth(BaseModel):
    status: str                   # "ok" | "degraded" | "down"
    latency_ms: float
    detail: Optional[str] = None


_uptime_start = time.perf_counter()


async def _check_db() -> ComponentHealth:
    """检查数据库连接"""
    start = time.perf_counter()
    try:
        async with get_db_session() as session:
            await session.execute("SELECT 1")
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        status = "ok" if latency < 500 else "degraded"
        return ComponentHealth(status=status, latency_ms=round(latency, 2))
    except Exception as e:
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        return ComponentHealth(
            status="down", latency_ms=round(latency, 2), detail=str(e)
        )


async def _check_redis() -> ComponentHealth:
    """检查 Redis 连接"""
    start = time.perf_counter()
    try:
        redis = await get_redis()
        await redis.ping()
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        return ComponentHealth(status="ok", latency_ms=round(latency, 2))
    except Exception as e:
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        return ComponentHealth(
            status="down", latency_ms=round(latency, 2), detail=str(e)
        )


async def _check_litellm() -> ComponentHealth:
    """检查 LiteLLM 代理健康状态"""
    import httpx
    start = time.perf_counter()
    try:
        async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:
            resp = await client.get(
                f"{os.getenv('LLM_GATEWAY_URL', 'http://litellm:4000')}/health",
                timeout=5,
            )
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        if resp.status_code == 200:
            return ComponentHealth(status="ok", latency_ms=round(latency, 2))
        return ComponentHealth(
            status="degraded", latency_ms=round(latency, 2),
            detail=f"HTTP {resp.status_code}"
        )
    except Exception as e:
        latency = (time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000
        return ComponentHealth(
            status="down", latency_ms=round(latency, 2), detail=str(e)
        )


# ── /health: 深度健康检查（包含所有依赖）──
@router.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    """详细健康检查：检查所有外部依赖"""
    db_check = await _check_db()
    redis_check = await _check_redis()
    litellm_check = await _check_litellm()

    component_statuses = {
        "db": db_check,
        "redis": redis_check,
        "litellm": litellm_check,
    }

    # 整体状态判定
    status_counts = {}
    for comp in component_statuses.values():
        status_counts[comp.status] = status_counts.get(comp.status, 0) + 1

    if status_counts.get("down", 0) > 0:
        overall_status = "unhealthy"
    elif status_counts.get("degraded", 0) > 0:
        overall_status = "degraded"
    else:
        overall_status = "healthy"

    return HealthStatus(
        status=overall_status,
        version=os.getenv("APP_VERSION", "1.0.0"),
        timestamp=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
        uptime_seconds=round(time.perf_counter() - _uptime_start, 2),
        checks=component_statuses,
    )


# ── /ready: 就绪检查（K8s Readiness Probe）──
@router.get("/ready")
async def ready_check():
    """就绪检查：服务是否可以接收流量"""
    db_check = await _check_db()
    redis_check = await _check_redis()

    if db_check.status == "down" or redis_check.status == "down":
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=503,
            detail={
                "ready": False,
                "reason": f"db={db_check.status}, redis={redis_check.status}",
            }
        )

    return {"ready": True}


# ── /live: 存活检查（K8s Liveness Probe）──
@router.get("/live")
async def live_check():
    """存活检查：进程是否存活（轻量）"""
    return {"alive": True, "uptime_seconds": round(time.perf_counter() - _uptime_start, 2)}
```

### 14.6 优雅关机与热更新

```python
# 文件: app/core/shutdown.py

import asyncio
import signal
import logging
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

from fastapi import FastAPI
from prometheus_client import generate_latest

logger = logging.getLogger("moling.shutdown")


@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """FastAPI 生命周期管理（替代 startup/shutdown 事件）"""
    # ── 启动阶段 ──
    logger.info("Application starting...")
    await init_connections()
    await warm_up_cache()
    logger.info("Application started successfully")

    yield  # 应用运行期间

    # ── 关闭阶段（优雅关机）──
    logger.info("Shutting down gracefully...")
    await graceful_shutdown()


async def init_connections():
    """初始化连接池"""
    # 连接池已在 app/core/database.py 中延迟初始化
    # 此处仅做健康确认
    pass


async def warm_up_cache():
    """预热缓存（可选）"""
    from app.core.cache import CacheProtection
    try:
        # 预热热点项目
        pass
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning("Cache warm-up failed (non-fatal)", extra={"error": str(e)})


async def graceful_shutdown():
    """优雅关机流程（最多等待 30 秒）"""
    shutdown_tasks = []

    # 1. 停止接受新请求（K8s 已通过 preStop hook 从 Service 摘除）
    logger.info("Step 1: Stopping new requests...")
    await asyncio.sleep(1)

    # 2. 等待正在处理的请求完成（最多 10 秒）
    logger.info("Step 2: Draining active requests...")
    shutdown_tasks.append(asyncio.create_task(wait_for_active_requests(timeout=10)))

    # 3. 关闭数据库连接池
    logger.info("Step 3: Closing DB pool...")
    shutdown_tasks.append(asyncio.create_task(close_db_pool()))

    # 4. 关闭 Redis 连接池
    logger.info("Step 4: Closing Redis pool...")
    shutdown_tasks.append(asyncio.create_task(close_redis_pool()))

    # 5. 关闭 HTTP 客户端
    logger.info("Step 5: Closing HTTP client...")
    shutdown_tasks.append(asyncio.create_task(close_http_client()))

    # 6. 推送最终指标
    logger.info("Step 6: Pushing final metrics...")
    push_final_metrics()

    # 并发执行所有关闭任务
    results = await asyncio.gather(*shutdown_tasks, return_exceptions=True)
    for i, result in enumerate(results):
        if isinstance(result, Exception):
            logger.error(f"Shutdown step {i + 1} failed", extra={"error": str(result)})

    logger.info("Graceful shutdown complete")


async def wait_for_active_requests(timeout: int = 10):
    """等待活动请求处理完成"""
    import gc
    deadline = asyncio.get_event_loop().time() + timeout
    while asyncio.get_event_loop().time() < deadline:
        gc.collect()
        await asyncio.sleep(0.5)


async def close_db_pool():
    """关闭数据库连接池"""
    try:
        from app.core.database import engine
        await engine.dispose()
        logger.info("DB pool closed")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("Failed to close DB pool", extra={"error": str(e)})


async def close_redis_pool():
    """关闭 Redis 连接池"""
    try:
        from app.core.cache import redis_client
        await redis_client.close()
        logger.info("Redis pool closed")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("Failed to close Redis pool", extra={"error": str(e)})


async def close_http_client():
    """关闭 HTTP 客户端"""
    try:
        from app.services.llm import http_client
        await http_client.aclose()
        logger.info("HTTP client closed")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error("Failed to close HTTP client", extra={"error": str(e)})


def push_final_metrics():
    """推送最终指标（如果使用 PushGateway）"""
    try:
        from prometheus_client import push_to_gateway
        push_to_gateway(
            os.getenv("PROMETHEUS_PUSHGATEWAY", "pushgateway.moling:9091"),
            job="moling-api-shutdown",
            registry=None,
        )
        logger.info("Final metrics pushed")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.warning("Failed to push final metrics", extra={"error": str(e)})
```

```yaml
# ── K8s PodDisruptionBudget ──
apiVersion: policy/v1
kind: PodDisruptionBudget
metadata:
  name: moling-api-pdb
  namespace: moling
spec:
  minAvailable: 1
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: moling
      component: api
```

### 14.7 数据备份与恢复

#### 14.7.1 PostgreSQL 备份策略

```bash
# 文件: scripts/backup-db.sh

#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# 墨灵数据库备份脚本
# 备份策略：
#   - 每日全量备份（凌晨 2:00）
#   - 每小时 WAL 归档（持续归档到 S3）
#   - 保留 7 天本地备份，30 天 S3 备份
# ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

BACKUP_DIR="${BACKUP_DIR:-/backup}"
S3_BUCKET="${S3_BUCKET:-s3://moling-backup}"
DB_NAME="${DB_NAME:-moling}"
DB_USER="${DB_USER:-moling}"
DATE=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
RETENTION_DAYS=7
S3_RETENTION_DAYS=30

export PGPASSWORD="${DB_PASSWORD:-moling_secret}"

# 创建备份目录
mkdir -p "${BACKUP_DIR}/${DATE}"

echo "[$(date)] Starting full backup..."

# 全量备份（使用自定义格式：支持并行压缩）
pg_dump \
  -h "${DB_HOST:-db}" \
  -U "${DB_USER}" \
  -d "${DB_NAME}" \
  -F custom \               # 自定义格式（可并行恢复）
  -j 4 \                     # 并行压缩（4 线程）
  -Z 9 \                     # 最大压缩级别
  -f "${BACKUP_DIR}/${DATE}/moling_full.dump"

echo "[$(date)] Full backup complete: ${BACKUP_DIR}/${DATE}/moling_full.dump"

# 备份元数据
pg_dump \
  -h "${DB_HOST:-db}" \
  -U "${DB_USER}" \
  -d "${DB_NAME}" \
  -s \                       # 仅 schema
  -f "${BACKUP_DIR}/${DATE}/moling_schema.sql"

echo "[$(date)] Schema backup complete"

# 同步到 S3
aws s3 sync "${BACKUP_DIR}" "${S3_BUCKET}/db/" \
  --storage-class STANDARD_IA

echo "[$(date)] Backup uploaded to S3"

# 清理本地超过保留期的备份
find "${BACKUP_DIR}" -maxdepth 1 -type d -mtime +${RETENTION_DAYS} -exec rm -rf {} \;
echo "[$(date)] Local cleanup complete (retention: ${RETENTION_DAYS}d)"

# 清理 S3 上超过保留期的备份
aws s3 ls "${S3_BUCKET}/db/" --recursive | while read -r line; do
  create_date=$(echo "$line" | awk '{print $1}')
  if [[ $(date -d "$create_date" +%s) -lt $(date -d "-${S3_RETENTION_DAYS} days" +%s) ]]; then
    file_path=$(echo "$line" | awk '{print $4}')
    aws s3 rm "${S3_BUCKET}/${file_path}"
  fi
done

echo "[$(date)] S3 cleanup complete (retention: ${S3_RETENTION_DAYS}d)"
echo "[$(date)] Backup finished successfully"
```

#### 14.7.2 WAL 持续归档配置

```conf
# 文件: deploy/postgres/archive.conf
# 在 postgresql.conf 中添加：

wal_level = replica                     # 需要 replica 以上级别
archive_mode = on                       # 开启归档
archive_command = 'aws s3 cp %p s3://moling-wal-archive/%f --storage-class STANDARD_IA'
archive_timeout = 60                    # 最多 60 秒归档一次
max_wal_size = 4GB                      # WAL 上限 4GB
min_wal_size = 1GB                      # WAL 最小保留 1GB

# 恢复配置
restore_command = 'aws s3 cp s3://moling-wal-archive/%f %p'
recovery_target_time = ''               # 可指定恢复到某个时间点
```

#### 14.7.3 RPO / RTO 目标

| 层级 | 数据保护 | RPO（最大数据丢失） | RTO（恢复时间） | 方法 |
|------|---------|-------------------|---------------|------|
| Level 0 | 全量备份 | 24h | 4h | pg_dump 每日全量 |
| Level 1 | WAL 归档 | 1h | 2h | 持续归档到 S3 |
| Level 2 | 同步复制 | 0（零丢失） | 5min | Patroni 同步复制 |
| Level 3 | 异地副本 | 5min | 15min | 异地 Patroni + WAL 流式 |

```bash
# 恢复流程脚本

# 文件: scripts/restore-db.sh
#!/bin/bash
set -euo pipefail

BACKUP_FILE="${1:-}"
RESTORE_DB="${RESTORE_DB:-moling_restored}"

if [ -z "${BACKUP_FILE}" ]; then
  echo "Usage: $0 <backup-file>"
  echo "Available backups:"
  aws s3 ls s3://moling-backup/db/ --recursive | grep ".dump$"
  exit 1
fi

echo "[$(date)] Starting restore from: ${BACKUP_FILE}"

# 1. 下载备份
aws s3 cp "${BACKUP_FILE}" /tmp/restore.dump

# 2. 创建临时数据库
createdb -U "${DB_USER}" "${RESTORE_DB}"

# 3. 恢复（并行恢复，4 线程）
pg_restore \
  -U "${DB_USER}" \
  -d "${RESTORE_DB}" \
  -j 4 \
  -v \
  /tmp/restore.dump

echo "[$(date)] Restore complete: ${RESTORE_DB}"

# 4. 验证
psql -U "${DB_USER}" -d "${RESTORE_DB}" -c "SELECT count(*) FROM projects;"
```

### 14.8 日志收集方案

#### 方案 A: Loki + Grafana（推荐，轻量级）

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/monitoring/loki-stack/docker-compose.yml
# 或 K8s Helm 配置

# 日志采集：Promtail（DaemonSet 模式）

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: moling-api
    static_configs:
      - targets: [localhost]
        labels:
          job: moling-api
          namespace: moling
          __path__: /var/log/moling/*.log

  - job_name: moling-k8s
    kubernetes_sd_configs:
      - role: pod
    pipeline_stages:
      - json: {}
    relabel_configs:
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_app]
        target_label: app
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_label_component]
        target_label: component
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace]
        target_label: namespace
      - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_name]
        target_label: pod
```

```
Loki 日志查询示例（LogQL）：

# 查询特定 trace_id 的所有日志
{app="moling-api"} |= `"trace_id": "a1b2c3d4e5f6..."`

# 查询最近 15 分钟的错误日志
{app="moling-api"} |= `"level": "ERROR"` |= `"code": 5`

# 查询慢 SQL 日志
{app="moling-api"} |= `"Slow SQL query detected"`

# 按错误码统计
sum by (code) (
  count_over_time(
    {app="moling-api"} |= `"code"` | pattern `"code": <code>` [5m]
  )
)
```

#### 方案 B: ELK Stack（功能丰富，资源开销较大）

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/monitoring/filebeat.yml

filebeat.inputs:
  - type: container
    paths:
      - /var/log/containers/*.log
    processors:
      - decode_json_fields:
          fields: ["message"]
          target: ""
          overwrite_keys: true

output.elasticsearch:
  hosts: ["${ELASTICSEARCH_HOST}:9200"]
  username: "${ELASTICSEARCH_USER}"
  password: "${ELASTICSEARCH_PASSWORD}"
  index: "moling-logs-%{+yyyy.MM.dd}"
  bulk_max_size: 1000

setup.kibana:
  host: "${KIBANA_HOST}:5601"

logging.level: info
```

### 14.9 Secret 管理方案

#### 方案一：K8s External Secrets + Vault（推荐生产环境）

```yaml
# 文件: deploy/k8s/external-secret.yaml

apiVersion: external-secrets.io/v1beta1
kind: ExternalSecret
metadata:
  name: moling-secrets
  namespace: moling
spec:
  refreshInterval: "1h"          # 每小时自动同步
  secretStoreRef:
    name: vault-backend
    kind: ClusterSecretStore
  target:
    name: moling-secrets          # 目标 K8s Secret 名称
    creationPolicy: Owner         # ESO 拥有该 Secret
  data:
    # 数据库
    - secretKey: DATABASE_URL
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/database
        property: url
    # Redis
    - secretKey: REDIS_URL
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/redis
        property: url
    # JWT
    - secretKey: JWT_SECRET
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/jwt
        property: secret
    # LLM API Keys
    - secretKey: OPENAI_API_KEY
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/llm
        property: openai_api_key
    - secretKey: ANTHROPIC_API_KEY
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/llm
        property: anthropic_api_key
    # 存储
    - secretKey: STORAGE_ACCESS_KEY
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/storage
        property: access_key
    - secretKey: STORAGE_SECRET_KEY
      remoteRef:
        key: moling/production/storage
        property: secret_key
```

#### 方案二：K8s Secret + Sealed Secrets（GitOps 友好）

```bash
# 使用 kubeseal 加密 Secret

# 1. 创建本地 Secret（仅用于加密，不提交）
kubectl create secret generic moling-secrets \
  --namespace moling \
  --from-literal=DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://... \
  --dry-run=client -o json > moling-secrets.json

# 2. 使用集群公钥加密
kubeseal --format=yaml < moling-secrets.json > sealed-secret.yaml

# 3. 提交 sealed-secret.yaml 到 Git（安全）
git add sealed-secret.yaml

# 4. 部署
kubectl apply -f sealed-secret.yaml
```

#### 方案三：环境变量（开发/小型部署）

```bash
# 文件: .env.production（不提交到 Git）
# 使用 sops 加密后提交

# sops --encrypt --age <AGE_PUBLIC_KEY> .env.production > .env.production.enc
# sops --decrypt .env.production.enc > .env.production

APP_NAME=墨灵 API
DEBUG=false
SECRET_KEY=${SECRET_KEY}

DATABASE_URL=postgresql+asyncpg://moling:${DB_PASSWORD}@db:5432/moling
REDIS_URL=redis://:${REDIS_PASSWORD}@redis:6379/0

JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
